(2) Li Meng-geng, Shang Yun-wu, Li Lang-yan, Huo Zhi-cheng, and Dong Shao-liang were elected to petition the Central Government. (3) It was decided to go to petition at 9:00 a.m. on the 13th.

Telegram Original

(1) Telegram to the National People: "It has been discovered that the Japanese and Koreans are conspiring to forcibly excavate farmland in Wanbaoshan, and have shot and killed our farmers and police. These brutal actions have reached their extreme. Furthermore, the Japanese have incited Koreans to massacre our overseas Chinese in Korea for days, with the number exceeding one thousand. Shops have been burned, and there have been attacks and looting. The situation is increasingly dire, causing our overseas Chinese to lose all protection of their lives and property. As a result, no fewer than ten thousand have fled back to the country or taken refuge in various consulates. The pitiful situation is unbearable to witness. Anyone with a shred of conscience, how can they endure this? Although the government has made serious protests, they show no sincerity and attempt to evade responsibility. Such disregard for humanity and cunning pursuit of wicked schemes makes them public enemies in the international community and vermin among rulers. All of us Chinese people should rise up and urge the government to engage in stern negotiations with them, vowing to achieve the goals of punishing the murderers, providing compensation and consolation, issuing apologies, and providing concrete guarantees that such incidents will not happen again. Better to be a broken jade than an intact tile; this is a crucial moment. This telegram is urgent, please take note." (2) Telegram to Deputy Commander Zhang and the Northeast Political Affairs Committee: "Recent newspapers have detailed reports and telegrams from various sources regarding the Wanbaoshan case. The Japanese incited Koreans to forcibly excavate civilian land, destroy roads, and build dikes. Japanese police then shot and killed our farmers and police. Our legitimate and inherent industries and our good and honest farmers have been subjected to brutal and inhumane treatment by these Japanese devils and Koreans who have lost their country and their homes, being slaughtered at will. Just speaking of it is enough to make one's hair stand on end. Furthermore, Koreans in Pyongyang, Incheon, and other places in Korea have been engaged in狂肆暴動 daily狂肆暴動, slaughtering overseas Chinese, burning and looting shops, destroying houses, and attacking markets. These are all organized acts of violence. The Japanese are covering their ears while stealing a bell. The intentions of Sima Zhao are clear to everyone. Such cruelty and inhumanity, disregarding humanity, law, international credibility, arbitrarily poisoning, and acting recklessly, have caused our farmers and overseas Chinese to lose all protection of their lives and property. Looking from afar at our homeland, our hearts are filled with pain. In addition to requesting the National Government to quickly order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to engage in serious negotiations, and not stop until the goals of punishing the murderers, providing compensation and consolation, issuing apologies, and providing concrete guarantees that such incidents will not happen again are achieved, we also request your committee to thoroughly investigate the cause of the incident, report it to the central government, and immediately arrest all the treacherous people such as Hao Yongde, punish them with the most severe punishments, to maintain law and order, and ensure the people's safety. This telegram is anxious, filled with urgent sincerity. Fellow villagers from the three northeastern provinces traveling in Beijing kowtow."

Petition

A petition concerning the Wanbaoshan case, which has caused suffering to overseas Chinese in Korea. We earnestly request your committee to forward a letter to the National Government quickly to engage in serious negotiations with Japan to maintain the people's lives and protect national rights. It has been discovered that in the Wanbaoshan area of Jilin, Korean residents have been driven by Japanese police to dig ditches and build dams without authorization, destroying our farmland, leading to conflicts with the local people. The fault lies with them, not with us. However, the newspapers of the Japanese Empire have falsely claimed that the Chinese are oppressing the Koreans, deliberately stirring up trouble. They have embellished the story, leading to the tragic anti-Chinese incidents throughout Korea. Looking eastward to Korea, we cannot help but feel grief and indignation. Our fellow villagers from the eastern provinces feel the pain most acutely. We deeply feel that this unfortunate event, having expanded to such an extent, cannot be resolved merely through verbal arguments or written telegrams. We must urgently seek a solution. Therefore, our association has convened fellow villagers and unanimously decided to request the central government to take the following actions: (1) Please send a letter to the National Government to announce the full details of this incident to all countries in the world, so that friendly nations can understand the truth and avoid being misled by the cunning propaganda of the Japanese. (2) The government should immediately implement all effective and necessary measures to protect overseas Chinese in various parts of Korea. (3) Please send a letter to the National Government to engage in serious negotiations with Japan, punish the rioters, provide compensation to the victims among the overseas Chinese, compensate for all losses, and provide conditional guarantees that similar incidents will not happen again in the future. (4) Please send a letter to the National Government ordering the Ministry of Interior to carefully plan for future matters such as Korean residents' naturalization or entry and residence in China, and instruct local governments in all provinces to strictly comply with these plans. (5) The Wanbaoshan tragedy was partly due to the deliberate instigation by Japan, but also due to the local treacherous people seeking profit. Please send a letter to the National Government ordering the Jilin Provincial Government to severely punish the treacherous people who caused the incident and instruct the provincial government to pay attention to various activities of Korean residents entering the country in the future, to prevent problems before they arise. The above points are the opinions of our association of fellow villagers after repeated consideration and unanimous decision. We specially submit this petition to your committee, requesting you to consider it and forward it to the National Government for quick implementation to protect the lives of overseas Chinese and preserve national rights. We are filled with fear and await your orders. Respectfully submitted to the Central Executive Committee, the Dongsan Province Association of Fellow Villagers in Beijing.

Lu Xun's View on Korean Anti-Chinese Sentiment

Report by the Qilu University Investigation Team

The Shandong Provincial Government Telegrams to Beijing requesting serious negotiations

Jinan Correspondence: The Wanbaoshan incident was in fact instigated by the Japanese. The Qilu University faculty and students jointly formed a goodwill investigation team, which arrived in Hanjing on July 1st. We have now received

Page 11

Summary of Important News

A telegram report stating that they have met with Zhang Weicheng, our country's Consul General in Korea. According to the discussion, the animosity between our people and Koreans has been deepening in recent years. There were originally 91,500 overseas Chinese residing in Korea, but the number has gradually decreased. The reasons are: (1) Overseas Chinese are hardworking and enduring, which has long been resented by Koreans. Recently, many Koreans have become unemployed, leading to restrictions on the entry of overseas Chinese, requiring registration and deliberately causing difficulties. (2) Chinese overseas Chinese in Korea are mostly engaged in the silk industry. Recently, the increase in tariffs has had a major impact. The ramie fabric industry initially earned 4-5 million yuan annually, but recently the Japanese have been promoting the use of ramie fabric woven by Taiwanese people and wearing colored clothes, leading to a decline in business. (3) Overseas Chinese lack education. There is only one small primary school inside the consulate in Hanjing, accommodating 170 students, and one after-school tutoring school. Few receive education, and knowledge inevitably lags behind. (4) Last year, the Northeast expelled communist Koreans, deepening the animosity between the two sides. It is fortunate that no accidents have occurred, etc. Unexpectedly, the Wanbaoshan incident occurred on July 2nd. However, the reasons for Korean anti-Chinese sentiment have been gradually building up.

The entire committee of the Shandong Provincial Government is extremely indignant about the Wanbaoshan case and immediately sent a telegram to Chairman Jiang of the National Government, requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to engage in serious negotiations. The telegram reads as follows: "To Chairman Jiang of the Nanjing National Government: It has been found that in the Jilin Wanbaoshan case, the Korean侨民 people were at fault for committing violence first, which is a disregard for public reason. However, according to newspaper reports, Korean civilians in Pyongyang, Yuan 산 and other places in Korea have been rioting for days, burning down Chinese shops and massacring overseas Chinese residents. It is clear that they were instigated by others, leading to this tragedy. All nationals share the same righteous indignation. We, who love our country and our people, dare not lag behind. We earnestly request your government to instruct the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to engage in serious negotiations with the Japanese side to stop the violence and provide relief. We are filled with fear and await your orders. Tengtian, Baisha, and Huangpi are successively recovered

The left wing of the annihilation of the Red Army captured Lichuan on the day. The right wing of the annihilation of the Red Army captured Huxi Yaotian and continues to search forward. The 19th Route Army is not far from Futian. The above places are all famous bandit nests, and Futian Donggu are located between Jishui and Ji'an, in a dangerous location. Central Committee and National Government Memorial Week

Fang Juehui Encourages Party Members to Intensify Work

Shao Yuanchong Discusses Central Government's Anti-Smoking Policy

Central Party Headquarters

On the morning of July 13th at 9:00 AM, the Central Party Headquarters held the 120th Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the auditorium. Central Committee members Ding Weifen, Fang Juehui, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Shao Lizi, Miao Peicheng, and others, as well as officials from various departments and guests, totaling about 500 people, attended. Chairman Ding Weifen presided. After the ceremony, Fang Juehui reported that the opening of the Fourth National Congress is less than three months away. During this period, all comrades of our party should reflect on the achievements and effects of party affairs and politics in the two years since the Third National Congress and should consider the extent to which party affairs and politics should develop after the Fourth National Congress, the benefits that the people should receive, and how to achieve this. In terms of past work, a few comrades have two shortcomings: one is laissez-faire, a lack of a sense of responsibility, which prevents the party's strength from being fully promoted; the other is romanticism, in which one's own environment is slightly stimulated, or one's aspirations are not satisfied, and a kind of divergent thought arises, often leading to misconduct. Therefore, before the upcoming Fourth National Congress, we must strictly examine ourselves and immediately correct our mistakes. Regarding the agenda of the Fourth National Congress, ten principles have been determined, which are of great importance, and it is necessary to actively study them beforehand. In terms of party affairs, we should focus on practical work, establish propaganda and news policies. In terms of politics, we should rectify national defense to resist foreign aggression and implement revolutionary diplomacy to restore national sovereignty. These are especially urgent needs of the times. All of our comrades should understand the danger of the country's position, concentrate their minds and talents with a spirit of striving and diligence, and engage in practical research so as to prepare rich materials and perfect plans for future contributions in order to achieve satisfactory results and create a new life in party affairs and politics. Regarding the suppression of bandits, Commander-in-Chief Chiang is supervising the advance in the front, determined to live and die with the people. All the soldiers under his command are united in their efforts to charge and break through the enemy lines. It is expected that the rebellious and rampant mob will be quickly wiped out. Commander-in-Chief Chiang also pays special attention to official governance during his military rule, strictly prohibiting corruption, because society as a whole depends on the support of the people. The people must have a common life and not be exploited by corrupt officials before the social organization can be sound, order can be stable, the scourge of the people can be eliminated, and the people's livelihood can be prosperous. Having obtained the way to rectify the root and clear the source, sweeping away the evil atmosphere is just a matter of time. It is hoped that the comrades in the rear will intensify their work during this critical period, just like the efforts during the conquest of Feng Yan last year. It would be even better if the comrades in various agencies could add one or two hours to their daily fixed working hours, etc. The meeting adjourned at 10:00 AM after the report.

National Government

On the morning of the same day at 10:00 AM, the National Government held Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Yu Youren, Cai Yuanpei, Shao Yuanchong, Shao Lizi, Ye Chucang, Zhu Peide, Ma Fuxiang, Zhu Lühe, Li Shuhua, Chen Bulei, Qian Changzhao, Wang Boqun, Gu Zhutong, and other government officials, totaling over 300 people, attended. Yu Youren presided. Shao Yuanchong spoke on the central government's anti-smoking policy, roughly saying that in recent weeks, the people of the country have paid close attention to the anti-smoking issue. A few weeks ago, a large batch of opium was transported from Guangdong, intending to transport it to various places for sale. Therefore, the Anti-Smoking Committee requested the Executive Yuan to establish inspection offices in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Fujian, but the implementation has not been very satisfactory. The domestic society and people have expressed suspicion and opposition. Later, the Anti-Smoking Committee, fearing that it would cause abuses, again requested the Executive Yuan to issue an order to abolish the inspection offices in various places. This matter has come to an end. The central government's established anti-smoking policy is unwavering. This time, due to the poor handling of the matter by the people in charge, the people have been suspicious, which shows that the people's expressions can be of great help to politics. The government will correct its political measures if it feels they are not entirely appropriate, and it can obtain the understanding of the people. The Fourth Plenary Session decided on four major tasks: cutting likin, suppressing bandits, eliminating communists, and prohibiting smoking. The first three items have been actively pursued, and cutting likin has already been achieved. As for the prohibition of smoking, the central government has not relaxed. The policy has not changed. This time, the establishment of the inspection office, or the comrades responsible for the prohibition of smoking, had different views, resulting in this organization. However, due to opposition from all sides, it was resolutely canceled to seek improvement. Since the Opium War a century ago, the people of the country have suffered deeply. Therefore, everyone advocates prohibition. The government is also absolutely responsible for handling it. Sun Yat-sen's last will and testament states: "The opium business can absolutely not coexist with the national government empowered by the people." At the National Anti-Smoking Conference in the 17th year, Chairman Chiang also expressed that the national government would never take a penny from opium. The people can supervise this. From the government's responsibility and Sun Yat-sen's last will and testament, the government will not change its anti-smoking purpose, compromise with opium, or say that China's finances are difficult, but can find ways in other areas, such as increasing the salt tax, which is much better. Increasing taxes will only make the people bear a little more tax burden, but it will not harm the future of the people or the nation. Otherwise, dyeing the national flag of the blue sky, white sun with the color of opium would be tearing up the spirit of the revolution and causing the nation to perish. The work of construction can be divided into two categories: active and passive. First, the active aspect is construction, which should focus on maintaining the lives of the people and the lives of the nation. Otherwise, even if education and livelihoods are well-managed, they will not last. Second, the passive aspect is eliminating harm. If opium cannot be prohibited, even if suppressing bandits is done, the people will not be able to have lasting peace. Now, the government is actively working on the four major tasks of the Fourth Plenary Session, such as cutting likin, suppressing bandits, and eliminating communists. It is also actively working on the prohibition of smoking to protect the lives of the people and consolidate the foundation of the country. In the past few weeks, due to the expression of opinions by the people, the central government has already canceled the inspection office. Some people in society still suspect that the government will change the name and continue to do so. The government's comrades responsible have stated that the prohibition of smoking is a determined purpose and will be firmly implemented. There will be no state trafficking or selling. Only in this way can we be worthy of the people who have been punished for anti-smoking laws. Some provinces have executed death sentences for smoking offenders, and they are still continuing to execute them. If the government is now easing up on the prohibition of smoking, those who were punished in the past would be wronged, and the government would be unfair. The revolutionary government, in order to establish itself in the world and show the spirit of a newly emerging country, should actively eliminate opium and complete the cause of saving the country. If there are still doubters, the government's responsible comrades should clearly state that the government is responsible for prohibiting smoking and will continue to do so according to the previous methods, and the criminal law and anti-smoking law cannot be changed during the period of implementation, and the anti-smoking laws cannot be changed by the second method. This can be told to the whole country, etc.

Chairman Yu Youren then gave a speech, roughly saying that since the Fourth Plenary Session, the government has paid extraordinary attention to the education cause, and educational reform is urgent. Therefore, the President of the Executive Yuan himself serves as Minister, which shows the government's emphasis on education. Minister Li has worked in the government for a long time, and his past work has been very diligent. This time, he is taking on the post of Minister and will be able to live up to the expectations of the national education community. Since the rise of the revolutionary army, there has been no actual reform of education. When Chairman Chiang served as Minister, although he had the intention of reform, he was unable to carry it out effectively due to the circumstances. However, the revolutionary cause is closely related to education. Therefore, the ability to succeed in education, reform, and construction is true success, true reform, and true construction. I hope that all comrades will strive to achieve the goal of actual reform. Commander Gu and the two division commanders Zhao and Li have been following the Commander-in-Chief for a long time. Commander Gu has put in a lot of effort in the revolutionary process. After taking office as Army Commander this time, he will be able to follow the great, strong, and healthy spirit and personality of the Commander-in-Chief, work hard, and make the army a model for the national army and make himself a model for soldiers. Next, Director of Education Li Shuhua replied, roughly saying that he will respectfully accept the speech of the Central Representative and Chairman. However, I am weak and incompetent and cannot be qualified for the job. I have repeatedly resigned to Chairman Chiang, but he did not allow it. Therefore, I will make an effort to take on the role. Education is the fundamental plan of the country, especially during the period of political tutelage, which is extremely important. In the future, I will follow Sun Yat-sen's last will and testament, the Provisional Constitution during the Period of Political Tutelage, the education facilities orientation plan decided by the National Assembly, and the aim of education of the Republic of China, under the guidance of the Party and the government, and the established regulations when Chairman Chiang served as Minister, and work hard on educational construction and improvement. I also hope that government comrades will provide guidance from time to time. Finally, Gu Zhutong replied, saying that after taking office, he will follow the instructions and work hard. After the reply, the ceremony was completed and the participants dispersed after taking a photo.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Kidnappers in Little Kunshan Arrested and Interrogated

Kidnapping cases have occurred in Little Kunshan. The County Public Security Bureau dispatched inspector Yang Shijie to secretly investigate. The night before, they received a report from a local informant named Xiao Zhou and arrested Ruan A'san (also known as Big Foot A'san), Xu Maozi, and Yang Xiaoxiang. They were taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation and confessed to the kidnapping of a person surnamed Da Pukang, Pan Fengde of Xi Jinggang, and a person surnamed Zhu of Mo Jiabang, and that they had all received a share of the loot. However, because the bandits' weapons had not been recovered, Inspector Yang received a secret order to continue searching in the countryside.

Bandit Leader Who Robbed Tianning Village Executed by Firing Squad

Tianning Village in Jiashan, Zhejiang Province, was robbed by bandits last year, resulting in significant losses. Subsequently, the Jiashan County Government arrested Hua Jinbiao (also known as Wang Jinbiao), the leader of the case. He confessed without denial. He was handed over to the Songjinjiapingtian County Bandit Suppression Headquarters for interrogation. It was determined that the bandit leader had colluded with a large gang and looted the entire town of Tianning Village, a heinous crime. He was sentenced to death. The Zhejiang Provincial Government approved the execution by telegram. Today (13th) at 1:00 PM, the bandit was brought in to verify his identity and tied to the execution ground at Yuhuang Pavilion and executed by firing squad.

County Executive Committee Distributes Positions

The County Party Department Executive Committee held its first executive committee meeting yesterday. Zhu Qianshan was elected as a Standing Committee member. As Zhu had not yet arrived in Songjiang, Lu Zhidao temporarily replaced him. Chen Youliang was approved as the General Affairs Officer, Jin Peihe as the Organization Officer, Qian Hao as the Training Officer, and Xu Xinmin as the Propaganda Officer. After the resolution was announced, they started working today.

Suzhou

Appeal of the Bribery Case of the Trial Officer Concluded

The case of Ju Bingpan, the former trial officer of Liuhe County, and the errand boy Liu Chi, who jointly defrauded money, was sentenced by the Jiang Ning Local Court. Ju Bingpan was sentenced to four years of imprisonment, and Liu Chi was sentenced to three years of imprisonment. Ju and Liu were not satisfied with the verdict and appealed to the High Court. The trial was concluded yesterday (13th) and will be sentenced on the 18th.

Third Mass Escape from the Reformatory

Due to poor management by the director Wang Yinruo, the Reformatory on 530 Road has already experienced two mass escapes of detainees. Unexpectedly, at 7:30 PM on the 12th, a third escape occurred. Taking advantage of the light rain, the detainees dug through the wall and escaped. By the time the guards found out and stopped them, 24 people had escaped. The Public Security Bureau was immediately notified and ordered to search for them. Seven people were apprehended at various locations outside Changmen and sent back to the facility for detention. The remaining escapees are still being searched for.

Collapse of the Old Changmen City Wall

The Suzhou city wall has been in disrepair for many years, and several sections are in a dangerous state. Yesterday (13th) at around 9:00 AM, the city wall near Tongzimen north of Old Changmen suddenly collapsed for about three zhang due to continuous heavy rain. The buildings of the Huaqingchi bathhouse near the city wall were also partially crushed. The police district in charge reported to the Public Security Bureau, which informed the Construction Bureau to repair it as soon as possible to strengthen the city's defense.

Chartered Steamship Temporarily Suspended

The County Government received a telegram from the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters stating that the 12 chartered gasoline ships would depart for Pengjiaqiao in Changshu to load soldiers who would be transported to Jiangxi for deployment. The Ministry of Military Affairs sent a section chief to Suzhou to negotiate. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Huang ordered the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau to charter six ships. Yesterday (13th), he summoned the person in charge of the Shipping Association to discuss chartering six ships to meet the needs. Later, he received a telegram stating that the steamships in Suzhou were not very suitable because the draft was more than two feet. Therefore, the chartering was temporarily suspended.

Wuxi

Thief Commits Arson in Attempt to Burn Down Lumber Company

Ling Ju-xing Lumber Company, located at the foot of the West City in Wuxi County, is known for its prosperous business. Around 9 o'clock the night before last, a thief surreptitiously entered through the back door and stole a coat and a flashlight. Before leaving, the thief set fire to a lean-to in the back, causing a sudden explosion of smoke and flames. Fortunately, the company employees noticed the fire and called for help. Various fire brigades arrived promptly and worked diligently to extinguish the blaze. However, the lean-to was completely destroyed by the fire.

Telephone Lines to Four Rural Townships Scheduled for Installation Tomorrow

Since taking office, Mao Feng, Director of the Wuxi County Construction Bureau, appointed Bei Qian as the telephone commissioner. Recently, Commissioner Bei resigned to take on another role and has submitted his resignation to Director Mao. Sun Jian, Director of the Department of Construction, appointed Yuan Fengxiang, a section member and engineer from the Telecommunications Administration Office's First Section, to come to Wuxi and take over the position. After being appointed, Yuan arrived in Wuxi the day before yesterday and met with Director Mao and Commissioner Zang the following day to discuss the implementation plan. Currently, a portion of the workers has already arrived in Wuxi from the town. The groundbreaking date is scheduled for the 15th, with the starting point for planting the poles being behind the Railway Hotel. Once the lines to the four rural townships are installed, they will be connected to the exchange.

Jiangyin

Opium Smuggling in Broad Daylight Amidst Anti-Smoking Campaign

Jiangyin is located on the Yangtze River and has always been known as an opium distribution center. Since the establishment of the Anti-Smoking Investigation Office, all sectors opposed it as being akin to a state-run opium monopoly. The Executive Yuan ordered its dissolution, and Shi Yunting, the Jiangyin Anti-Smoking Commissioner, has already concluded his work. However, the Northern Outer Investigation Office remains in existence, with rumors of reorganization. Amidst this anti-smoking campaign, on the morning of the 11th, a boat from Taizi in Jiangbei arrived at the Pu Hui Bridge outside the North Gate carrying a large quantity of opium, approximately 200 catties. The opium was unloaded publicly at the location, with armed guards providing protection. It is said that the opium was transported to Hexi and Junshan Lane.

Catholic Church Encroachment on Canal Land

On March 2, 1928, the Qingyang Catholic Church built a revetment that encroached on the canal. Local groups repeatedly opposed this, and the county government ordered the church to demolish the structure and restore the land, but the order has not been followed for nearly three years. Recently, Liu Chongyi, a representative of the church, filed an appeal with the Construction Department. The Construction Department decided that the church should demolish two feet of the structure. Qingyang party and government agencies believe that an appeal can only be filed within 30 days of the issuance of a disposal order. The county government's order to the church to demolish the structure was issued more than two years ago. The basis upon which the Construction Department accepted this appeal is questionable. Furthermore, when the Construction Bureau went to the countryside to measure the canal, it based its measurements on the dimensions of the old canal engineering drawings, confirming that the church had encroached on the canal by seven or eight feet. The villagers continue to oppose this and have also requested that the relevant authorities file an appeal.

Changzhou

Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad

Jing Peiyin, the son of a wealthy resident of Dingqiao Town in Danyang, Jing Jisheng, was kidnapped on February 9, 1929, while studying at a school in Wujin County. After school, on his way home, he was abducted by bandits. He was later killed when a ransom of 25,000 yuan was not paid. In March of the same year, Qi Zhihai, the son of Qi Qianlin from Xuanjiazhuang in the Third District of Wuyi County, was kidnapped while teaching in the village. He cried for help along the way and was shot by the bandits, dying shortly thereafter. Eight kidnappers involved in both cases, including Yuan Xiaoheshang and Wu Bolin, were apprehended by the Wudan Joint Defense Association, handed over to the county and transferred to the county court. After trial, Yuan Xiaoheshang and Wu Bolin were sentenced to death. The sentence was submitted to the Higher Court of Tian, and then reported to the provincial government for approval. Upon receiving the order, the county court retrieved the two convicts from prison at around 1 p.m. on the 12th, verified their identities, and dispatched police to take them to Fengweidun for execution by firing squad.

Stone Pillar Collapses, Crushing Boat Crew Member

On the 12th, a coal boat (owned by Zhao Hongtai) arrived at the Twelve-Bay area outside the West Gate of Wuyi County, across the river from the Great King Temple, having loaded coal in Shandong for unloading in Wuxi. During its return journey and passing through the area, it prepared to stop and rest. Crew member Liu Xitong, due to the strong winds and waves causing the boat to rock, tied one end of a rope to the boat and the other end to a stone pillar standing on the shore. Unfortunately, at that moment, the stone pillar collapsed, and Liu Xitong's legs were crushed beneath the pillar, while his head was submerged in the water. By the time the boat owner went to rescue him, Liu had already died.

Zhenjiang

Various Agencies Compete for Jiedi Nunnery

The Jiedi Nunnery, located at Gangzixia outside the South Gate of the county, is involved in a murder case and legal proceedings. The abbess, Decheng, has fled, and the nunnery site is abandoned and dilapidated due to the lack of management. Local agencies and organizations, seeking office space or locations for public undertakings due to inadequate facilities or difficulty finding premises, all intend to temporarily use the nunnery. Previously, the county-run Forest Farm had requested the county to designate the nunnery as its office after the murder case occurred. Subsequently, the Buddhist Association, based on letters from citizens, stated that the nunnery was unattended after Decheng's departure and requested that a monk be appointed to take charge. After discussion, it was decided to appoint De Tang, a monk from Jinshan Jiangtian Temple, as the abbot to manage the property. The county government dispatched personnel to investigate and consult with local residents to determine their opinions and report back truthfully for a decision. It is reported that in addition to the Forest Farm's intention to temporarily use the nunnery site, the Education Bureau intends to use it to establish a small school, the Security Corps intends to use it to establish a branch, and the First Autonomous Division intends to use it for offices. The final disposition of the nunnery will depend on the consensus of local residents and the approval of the county magistrate.

Yangzhou

Request to Arrest Liu Minzhai

Deng, the Director of the Jinan Salt Field, reported that the Yu Tong Salt Company's field stores were facing starvation due to the failure of the Yangzhou manager, Liu Minzhai, to provide relief, which led to a violent uprising. The report was submitted to Wang Zhanghu, the Director of the Lianghuai Salt Transport Department, who then telegraphed the Jiangdu County government yesterday to arrest Liu nearby and force him to remit the withheld funds to the field to alleviate the crisis.

Teachers and Staff to Again Jointly Demand Salaries

Jiangdu's education funding has been in arrears for several months. County Magistrate Chen initially planned to issue 60,000 yuan in loan certificates in the hope of settling accounts with teachers and staff by July 15 to clear the arrears. Today is the 13th, and the teachers and staff, seeing no progress, convened a meeting today to inquire with the county government and education bureau about the situation. However, it is reported that the county government is unable to raise enough funds through loan certificates. Furthermore, the heavy rains this week have blocked roads, preventing the collection of taxes and levies. The previously scheduled July 15 settlement is unlikely to occur.

City Wall Collapses, Injuring Elderly Woman

After more than ten days of continuous rain, the streets and alleys are flooded, and the disaster in the southern countryside is expanding. Xuejiazhai, Diaojiamiao, Qinqiaqiao, Xinhewan, Xifangqiao, and Dongjiatao dikes have all been submerged. The high-lying fields in the northwest and the early rice in the eastern countryside have also been inundated by the rain, and countless walls and houses have collapsed. Many villagers have come to the city to report the disaster. Yesterday (the 11th), the county ordered the Finance Bureau to investigate. Furthermore, yesterday afternoon (the 12th), several tens of yards of the city wall behind the electric plant outside the Customs Gate collapsed, crushing several nearby thatched houses and injuring an elderly woman.

Nantong

Severe Storm Causes Drastic Riverbank Collapse

The continuous wind and rain in Tongyi have caused the collapse of dikes and embankments along the river, with the erosion being extremely severe. To protect against tidal surges, the dikes rely on retreating banks. The Construction Department has approved the local request to establish the Lower Yangtze Northern Bank Erosion Prevention Association in Tongyi to plan and implement erosion prevention projects. The required funding, in addition to provincial and county allocations, will also be requested from the National Government for subsidies. Currently, the emergency reinforcement project for the Jiang'an Riverbank at the junction of Tong and Ru is being handled by the Construction Bureau.

Relief Center Requests Levy on Feast Donations

The Nantong Relief Center was previously ordered by the province to allocate Zhang Qian's assets as operating funds. Now that all of Zhang's assets have been returned, a request has been submitted to the county government for onward transmission to the province to approve the levy of 2% on feast donations to fund the vocational training center for vagrants.

Pinghu

Pawnshop Robbed, Handling of Aftermath

Yang Xilao, the chairman of the Zhapu Town Chamber of Commerce, submitted a report to the county government stating that after the Zhapu Guangji Pawnshop was looted by mutinous soldiers, the Chamber of Commerce dispatched Ye Liangfu and others to the pawnshop for inventory. A total of 136 items were stolen, with a total loan value of 447.8 yuan. The pawnshop has submitted a detailed list. After investigation, all of the stolen items belonged to pledgers and were not yet due. The report requested instructions from the county government to report to the province for guidance on how to handle the matter. The county government has submitted the report to the province for review. In the meantime, a notice has been posted stating that until further instructions are received from the province, pledgers are not allowed to cause any disturbances when the pawnshop reopens.

Bengbu

Conditions of the Bengbu Flood

Since the onset of the rainy season, continuous heavy rain has caused the Zhun River to rise sharply, almost reaching the banks. A section of the dike on the north bank of the Hebei River collapsed yesterday due to the flood, resulting in widespread flooding. The waves in the river are turbulent, capsizing several small boats. The Xiaobengbu area of Hebei is entirely submerged in water. The Eastern Playground and the northern ends of Guozhi Street and Guoqing Street in the city center are several feet deep in water, and most of the houses have been flooded. Hundreds of thatched houses have collapsed, with small boats floating among them, ferrying refugees. The Yongji Pawnshop at the northern end of Guozhi Street is several feet deep in water, and the wooden shelves and pledged clothing have been soaked. Pawn operations have been suspended immediately. The area around the Western Playground, near the boat pond, is even more severely flooded, with the low-lying areas turned into swamps. Small boats are navigating the area as if it were a lake. The New Great Road and the Ma'anzha on Taiping Street and Zhongzheng Street are flooded, with shops on both sides submerged. Laborers wade through the water, with the shallow areas reaching their knees and the deeper areas reaching their waists. The water is several feet deep at the floor of the Telegraph Bureau on Mujang Street, making it impossible for the staff to stay. The office was temporarily moved to the Dongya Hotel on Erma Street yesterday. The district branches of the Public Security Bureau surveyed the flood victims and counted more than 5,500 people. The victims in Hebei were not included in this count, and the total is estimated to be more than 7,000, displaced and in dire need of assistance. The Public Security Bureau, recognizing the severity of the disaster and the refugees' desperate need for food, initiated a relief effort and convened a meeting of all sectors at the bureau at 3 p.m. on the 11th to discuss relief measures, resulting in four resolutions.

Letter

Letter from Prosecutor Da Shiying of the Wuhu District Court

To the Esteemed Editor:

I am writing regarding an article in the "Foreign News" section of your newspaper on July 4 entitled "Major Uproar in Wuhu Legal Circles," which contains many inaccuracies. I am writing to request corrections to the following points:

(1) The cases involving the assault on Xu Shaolou and the injuries to Peng Qingsong at the Star Theater were both handled by Prosecutor Pei and have no connection to me. It is inappropriate to list Pei Xiyu and Da Shiying together. This is the first correction I request.

(2) Li Weixin was a judge in the Wuhu court before and worked with me for only ten days in June of last year before being transferred. I have never met Yu Hongming. There is no possibility of collusion. This is the second correction I request.

(3) With regard to the proposal by lawyer Sheng Liangzu that Han Lantian be investigated for bribery in connection with opium trafficking, I have already submitted a request to higher authorities to thoroughly investigate whether there was any bribery. The truth will eventually come out. Until the investigation is complete, no one should be arbitrarily slandered. This is the third correction I request.

Your newspaper is a model for the press, and I am concerned about the potential for confusion. Therefore, I am writing to request that you investigate and make the necessary corrections. I offer my sincere regards.

Da Shiying, Prosecutor of the Wuhu District Court, July 11

Educational News

Local

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Submits Report to Ministry on Results of Provisional Standards for Elementary School Curriculum Trial

The provisional standards for primary and secondary school curricula have been in effect for over a year since the Ministry of Education promulgated the trial requirement. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education established a Research Committee on Primary and Secondary School Curriculum Standards. The bureau has convened meetings to discuss the results of the trial and has compiled the reports from various primary and secondary schools in the city. The elementary school portion has now been completed and submitted to the ministry. The full text is as follows:

Report on the Results of the Trial of Provisional Standards for Elementary School Curriculum in Shanghai

Chinese Language

丨Teaching Time丨

(1) The weekly teaching time for Chinese language in each grade of elementary school seems too short and should be increased appropriately. "Reason": Following the teaching time stipulated in the provisional standards, the minimum requirements were often not met by the end of the curriculum.

丨Assignment Requirements丨

(1) The requirement to learn simplified running script in the writing section of Chinese language for grades three and four should be deleted. "Reason": 1. Children in grades three and four have not yet mastered regular script, and practicing running script will hinder their progress in regular script. 2. Children in grades three and four do not have a clear understanding of the shape of regular script characters. Learning running script will reduce the accuracy of their writing of regular script (Fifth-grade children make more mistakes after learning running script than before. This is true for fifth-grade children, let alone third and fourth-grade children).

(2) Learning running script should be moved to grades five and six.

(3) In the Chinese language assignment requirements for the third grade, the only aspect students focus on is the type of character. According to the teachers, in addition to the type of character, students should also pay attention to the writing tool used. There are two main types:

1. Soft brush. 2. Hard pen. Soft brush refers to the traditional brush, while hard pen refers to fountain pens, pencils, etc. Elementary schools often think that formal writing refers only to learning with a soft brush, which is a traditional habit. The reason for writing in elementary school is that it is necessary for life in society. In the past, the need was for characters written with soft brushes (i.e., brush calligraphy), but the current need is for characters written with hard pens. If we continue to teach writing as before, using only soft brushes and not hard pens, it would be a serious mistake. Although the learning of regular, semi-cursive, small characters in elementary Chinese writing does not explicitly limit the use of a specific soft or hard pen, it can be freely used. However, to prevent misunderstanding and for clarity, the writing tool should also be specified. The writing requirements for each grade can be modified as follows:

1. First and second grades: 1. The original "writing of announcements and signs" can be changed to "writing of announcements and signs with soft or hard pen." 2. The original "practice of writing simple familiar characters" can be changed to "practice of writing simple familiar characters with soft or hard pen." 3. The original "design practice of other writing" can be changed to "design practice of other calligraphy with soft or hard pen."

2. Third and fourth grades: 1. The original "writing of announcements, signs, letters, and notes, etc." can be changed to "writing of announcements, signs, letters, and notes, etc. with soft or hard pen." 2. The original "practice of regular script middle characters" can be changed to "practice of regular script middle characters with soft brush" and "practice of regular script small characters with soft or hard pen." 3. The original "learning to write simple running script" can be changed to "learning to write simple running script with soft or hard pen."

3. Fifth and sixth grades: 1. The original "writing of practical texts" can be changed to "writing of practical texts with soft or hard pen." 2. The original is the same as the second item for the third and fourth grades, so the modification can be the same. 3. The original "practice of writing simple running script middle and small characters" can be changed to "practice of writing simple running script middle characters with soft brush" and "practice of writing simple running script small characters with soft or hard pen." In short, the words "soft brush" or "hard pen" should be added to words like "practice" and "learn." Otherwise, it should be noted in the annotations.

(4) Recognition of common simplified, irregular, and seal script characters should be moved to grades five and six. Children in grades three and four do not yet have a correct understanding of characters and should focus on simplicity and avoid complexity.

(5) The "recognition of phonetic symbols" should be added to the assignment requirements for reading in the first and second grades. "Reason": Phonetic symbols are an important tool for helping to recognize Chinese characters. Based on the actual situation, children in grades one and two are already able to recognize them.

丨Minimum Standard丨

(1) The "ability to write running script" should be removed from the minimum standard for the primary level.

Party Doctrine

(1) Party doctrine in lower grades can be combined with society and nature to form a "common sense" subject. "Reason": The general explanation contains a clause that includes teaching material on the Three Principles of the People, which is quite broad. If party doctrine is made an independent subject with systematic study, it would be too far removed from children's experiences. If teaching materials are selected based on children's needs, it will conflict with other subjects.

Social Studies

丨Assignment Requirements丨

(1) A career guidance item should be added to the social studies assignment requirements for the higher grades. "Reason": Based on the actual situation, few elementary school graduates continue their education, while many enter the workforce. Therefore, career guidance should be provided to prepare them for employment.

丨Minimum Standard丨

(1) The provisional curriculum standards state that "except for party doctrine, which is administered by the Central Party Department's Training Department, the remaining subjects are drafted, compiled, and organized by experts commissioned by the Ministry of Education's Primary and Secondary School Curriculum Standards Drafting Committee." Based on this, party doctrine is a separate subject equal to social studies and is not included within social studies.

The social studies minimum standard for the fifth grade, (1) the end of the primary level, includes "(4) the key points of practicing four rights... (5) understanding the key points of five rights and four rights." According to teachers, these materials should be placed in party doctrine and not mixed into social studies. Strictly speaking, party doctrine is a kind of social studies, but now we are building the country based on the Three Principles of the People, which is more important than any other subject. Because it is important, it should be separated from social studies to become an independent subject for special study. Since party doctrine is separated from social studies to become an independent subject for special study, all content related to party doctrine should be placed within the scope of party doctrine to avoid confusion and repetition.

The following should be added to the requirements for senior graduation: "Understanding the general situation of the world's countries and China's position in the world."

Arithmetic

丨Assignment Requirements丨

(1) Proficiency in arithmetic, whether through written calculation or abacus, requires continuous practice over a long period. The weekly time allocated in the assignment requirements for the higher grades is actually too short.

(2) In the arithmetic requirements for the first and second grades, the recognition of days, weeks, months, and years should be moved to at least the sixth item, "Recognition of numbers 10 to 19," with the exception of the week item. Because the numbers used to represent days, months, and years are often greater than the numbers 1 to 9.

(3) Simple bookkeeping (for personal and family use) should be added to the assignment requirements for the third and fourth grades. "Reason": To enable children to understand the use and recording methods of accounting books.

(4) Regarding arithmetic, (1) The meaning of terms such as square inch, square foot, cubic inch, cubic foot, etc., are difficult for children to understand. According to teachers, the teaching material related to squares in the arithmetic assignment requirements for the third grade should be moved from the first and second grades to the third and fourth grades. The teaching material related to cubes should be moved from the third and fourth grades to the fifth and sixth grades.

丨Key Points of Teaching Method丨

(1) Teaching abacus and written calculation separately is better than teaching them together. "Reason": (1) Learning the abacus is more difficult than learning written calculation. (2) It is inconvenient to have an abacus on the desk while learning. (3) It is not easy for teachers to identify children's mistakes when learning abacus and written calculation at the same time.

Practical Arts

丨Assignment Categories丨

The second assignment category of elementary school practical arts is divided into (1) school affairs, (2) household chores, (3) agricultural affairs, (4) crafts, and (5) business conditions, encompassing agriculture, industry, commerce, and academics. In terms of content, it can be said to be extremely complete. In terms of scope, it can be said to be extremely broad. However, it is difficult to hire a teacher capable of handling such a wide range of tasks. If the tasks are assigned separately, elementary school courses will become more scattered than before, which is contrary to the original intention of compiling the curriculum standards.

丨Difficult Problems with Practical Arts丨

It is difficult to investigate the results of household chores and family operations, and the results obtained are not accurate. Cooking practice is difficult to maintain order due to the large number of students and the insufficient supply of utensils. Furthermore, animal husbandry and crop cultivation are difficult to implement due to limited school grounds.

Nature Studies

丨Minimum Standard丨

(1) The fifth minimum standard of elementary nature study, (1) at the end of the primary level, "(2) understanding the general function of various daily necessities for clothing, food, housing, and transportation" includes many various daily necessities for clothing, food, housing, and transportation. It seems a little too advanced to understand all of them at the end of the primary level. According to the teachers, this item can refer to the method of "(3) having more than eight good hygiene habits" and limit the number to be more appropriate.

(2) The fifth minimum standard of elementary nature study, (2) there are a total of seven items for senior graduation. Among the seven items, only (1) and (2) are related to nature, while (3), (4), (5), (6), and (7) are related to hygiene. Formally, it seems to be too biased toward hygiene. According to the teachers, another item can be added to the nature aspect, which is to understand the general functions of the various daily necessities for clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and increase the number compared to the end of the primary level, referring to the method of good hygiene habits.

Music Department

丨Work Items丨

(1) In the first and second grades, it is advisable to add the recognition of "preliminary music flashcards" to the practice items. Because students in the first and second grades basically do not use musical scores when singing, they must at least have a preliminary understanding of the musical score so as to prepare for sight-singing in the third and fourth grades. As for the flashcards, the teacher should make them by himself, for example, write 丨 on the front and a quarter note on the back, etc.

丨There are three points about music丨

(2) The reading method of the Gongche notation and the beat can be changed to the fifth grade, and combined with the teaching of playing Chinese musical instruments. Children in the third and fourth grades are just beginning to practice reading regular scores, and they really don't have the energy and time to study the Gongche notation. If it is changed to the fifth grade to study, it can be combined with the performance of Chinese music, on the one hand to make children feel the need to learn, and on the other hand to give children the opportunity to apply and practice.

(3) Two-part rounds can be practiced earlier. Two-part round practice is not a difficult task, and can be started as early as the third and fourth grades to increase children's interest in music. Undoubtedly, children will be incredibly excited to hear this novel way of singing and beautiful harmony.

(4) The performance of Chinese musical instruments should be included in the practice column of the work items for the fifth and sixth grades. Playing Chinese musical instruments is indeed a matter that primary school students should practice. Even the minimum and maximum graduation standards stipulated in the standard clearly state that they should be able to use two or more kinds of Chinese musical instruments, but not a single sentence is mentioned in the work items. It is best to add it.

Physical Education Department

丨Work Category丨

Extracurricular activities are best not held at noon, because it is too close to lunchtime, which is not very suitable for hygiene.

丨Work Items for Each Grade丨

In the third and fourth grade sports item, there are simple ball sports, so simple track and field sports can of course also be included.

丨Key Points of Teaching Methods丨

1. The race distances in the athletes' sports meet item list still use the yard system. It is found that the World Far East National University and Middle School Games have all been changed to the metric system. For the sake of consistent connection, it is necessary to change yards to meters. 2. The low hurdle should be set at 110 meters. It has been found to be applicable after experiments in the Shanghai City Primary School Joint Sports Meet. However, Group B seems to be canceled.

Subject Combination

1. Music and Physical Education, 2. Crafts and Art, 3. Personal Hygiene and Public Hygiene.

(1) Music and physical education in lower grades can be combined into "singing and games." Teaching music and physical education as two separate subjects in lower grades is too uninteresting and boring. It seems necessary to combine them in accordance with the principle that primary school subjects should not be too numerous.

(2) Combining crafts and art teaching in lower grades is more convenient. "Reason": In order to facilitate production in lower-grade crafts, it is necessary to first understand the concept of image. On the one hand, it is easy to arouse interest in studying art, and on the other hand, it can be applied to production. The combination of the two sides is more interesting, so it seems more convenient to combine teaching.

(3) Personal hygiene and public hygiene should be combined for teaching, which is more convenient.

"Reasons": 1. In this standard, the personal hygiene item belongs to the natural science subject, and the public hygiene belongs to the social science subject. Since the experiment, it has been found that personal hygiene and public hygiene are related everywhere. It is quite inconvenient to teach them separately. 2. The people of our country have always neglected hygiene. Elementary education should try its best to instill and cultivate knowledge and habits of hygiene. Now that it is divided into natural and social sciences for teaching, it is inevitable that there will be some bias, which is not the way to pay attention to hygiene.

"Measures": 1. Public hygiene in social science is incorporated into the natural science under the hygiene intelligence item. Teaching is combined with geography and history, called social science. Combined with natural phenomena, life needs, and hygiene intelligence (public hygiene and personal hygiene), it is called natural science. The amount of time is changed to:

Natural lower grade 120 minutes, middle grade 150 minutes, higher grade 180 minutes.

Social lower grade 60 minutes, middle grade 90 minutes, higher grade 150 minutes.

2. The public hygiene in social science and the personal hygiene in natural science are separated and combined, called hygiene. A special subject is set up, and the weekly teaching time for each grade is set at 60 minutes. (End)
