Local News

All Circles in This City Held Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Congress Yesterday

Resolved to Sever Economic Relations with Japan

Joint Committee Organized by All Circles

Andong is in Emergency, Materials and Food are Exhausted

All circles in this city held an anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese congress at the City Chamber of Commerce at 3 pm yesterday for the Korean people's anti-Chinese riots. It was resolved to issue a declaration and organize the Shanghai All Circles Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee. There were eight proposals, and all other proposals were handed over to the committee for handling. The situation yesterday is recorded below.

Attending Groups

The groups that participated in the congress yesterday included Party Headquarters of District 12345678910 and their branches, and the labor circles included the Knitting Industry Union, Printing Industry Union, Tooth and Bone Utensil Industry Union, Ink Industry Union, Pig Bristle Industry Union, Water and Electricity Industry Union, Cigarette Industry Union, Dyeing Industry Union, Publishing Industry Union, Silk Reeling Industry Union, Postal Workers' Union, Silk Weaving Industry Union, etc. The business circles included the City Chamber of Commerce, Cigarette Association, Tobacco Exchange Association, Nail Industry Association, Cotton Cloth Association, New Medicine Association, Shanghai Korean Association, etc. The academic circles included the Cultural College, Education Associations of District 123456, the Citizens' Federation, the Guannan Group Federation, the Diplomatic Support Association for the Netherlands, the National Goods Maintenance Association, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, the Taxpayer Chinese Association, and more than 500 other organizations. The representatives were Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Zheng Chengqing, Tao Baichuan, and more than 1,000 others.

Meeting Order

(1) Opening of the meeting, (2) Public election of the temporary presidium, (3) All stand up, (4) Bow three times to the Party National Flag and the Prime Minister's portrait, (5) Xue reads the Prime Minister's will, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speeches by representatives from all walks of life, (8) Adoption of the declaration, (9) Discussion, (10) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report

Wang Yansong, Zheng Chengqing, Wang Wenhua, Li Yongxiang, Tao Baichuan and other five people were elected as the presidium. The master of ceremonies was Xu Yefu, and the recorders were Xue Guangqian and Zhao Shusen. Chairman Zheng Chengqing reported that, everyone, today all circles in this city are holding an anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese congress to discuss the Wanbaoshan case and the Korean massacre of overseas Chinese. Brothers feel very sad. The occurrence of the Wanbaoshan case, on the surface, was caused by a very small reason, arising from the Korean people's strong planting of paddy fields. However, upon closer observation, it was the beginning of the Japanese imperialism's implementation of the active policy of Manchuria and Mongolia. Observing its every move to instigate the Korean people's violence, there was sufficient preparation beforehand and a consistent policy afterwards. As for why the Japanese imperialism dared to risk the world's disapproval and easily stirred up disputes between China and Japan, as seen by brothers, there are four major long-term causes: (1) Changes in diplomatic policy. When Shidehara first took office as Foreign Minister, his diplomatic policy towards China was a stable diplomacy, expressing goodwill towards China everywhere. Later, he was fiercely attacked by the domestic opposition party, accusing him of being weak and incompetent. In order to cater to the people's hearts and ease the opposition, the diplomatic policy towards China was changed to active aggression. (2) Dealing with the Soviet Russia's Five-Year Plan. The Soviet Russia's Five-Year Plan is no different from a plan to fight against Japan. In order to prepare to deal with it, Japan had to first seek to seize the Northeast and make arrangements in advance. Therefore, it used the Wanbaoshan case as an excuse to send troops to the Northeast to fulfill its ambitions. (3) Alienating the feelings between China and Korea. China and Japan will inevitably have a war. If the Korean people's hearts are not towards Japan, when Japan sends troops to the East Province, the Korean people will create disturbances and rebellions in the rear, attacking from both sides, which will be enough to put the Japanese people to death. Therefore, they do not hesitate to alienate and provoke from the side, creating deep-seated animosity between the two sides, with no opportunity to join hands and help each other. (4) Relieving domestic unemployment problems. The state of Japan's recession is known to all. Recently, in order to relieve domestic unemployment problems, they have driven the Korean people to our Northeast territory and transplanted their people to Korea. Based on the above reasons, it can be seen that the Wanbaoshan and Korean cases are actually the background of the Japanese people's violence, and their nature is more serious than the Jinan Massacre. However, the diplomatic authorities of our country clearly know that the incident has expanded and the situation is serious. Although protests have been filed, the results are still unknown. If the victims were easily replaced by the people of other countries, their respective governments would have not only filed serious protests long ago, but also sent troops to protect them. Now that the matter is so serious, and the lives of overseas Chinese are so precarious, according to reports, in Seoul, Incheon, Pyongyang, Sinuiju, and other places in Korea, Korean rioters have expelled overseas Chinese from the country, and countless old and young overseas Chinese have died and been injured. The Japanese police have claimed that they cannot be responsible for local security. Overseas Chinese have left the country to return to their homeland. As of the day before yesterday, more than 5,000 people have entered the country through Andong, and more than 10,000 other refugees have wandered and sought refuge, extremely embarrassed. How should we feel about this situation? On the one hand, we still hope that the government will implement the diplomacy of the association and seriously negotiate with Japan. On the other hand, the people of the country should rise up together, with one heart and one mind, to be the backing of the government's negotiations, and immediately engage in economic severance with the country. Hopefully, all colleagues from all walks of life present will discuss appropriate methods to maintain the lives of overseas Chinese and determine the policy towards Japan.

Representative Report

Liu Zihong, representative of the Shanghai Korean Association, reported the process, briefly saying that since the Wanbaoshan incident, the local Japanese military and police not only did not stop the Korean people's violent behavior, but instead opened fire to demonstrate and protect and instigate them to proceed. The Korean people relied on their amulets and acted recklessly. Japanese newspapers deliberately provoked with ulterior motives, which led to the expansion of the storm and spread throughout Korea. General rioters rose up in response, gathered crowds to hate the Chinese, and indulged in ferocity. All Chinese businessmen in major commercial districts such as Seoul, Incheon, Wonsan, Busan, and Pyongyang were harmed together, and their property and lives were destroyed. Deaths and injuries were numerous and tragic. Even cutting hearts and digging eyes, throwing them on the road, all kinds of cruelty, were exhausted. The world was dark, and there was nothing like it in ancient times. The actual situation at that time is recorded below. (1) When the rioters launched an attack on Chinatown in Incheon, the momentum was fierce and extremely critical. Fortunately, the British consul came out to uphold justice and began to restrain the traces. Otherwise, thousands of overseas Chinese in Chinatown would have been spared. (2) When the rioters brutally killed overseas Chinese, there were originally one or two proper Koreans who issued leaflets to persuade them to stop. However, they were prevented from distributing them by the Japanese police, which led to the spread of brutal violence throughout Korea. Then the Japanese people's intention to help evil is self-evident. (3) When the Pyongyang riot was at its worst, overseas Chinese gathered at the station, eager to escape. However, the train refused to load them, which led to no way to escape. Then the Japanese people's prior secret agreement was obvious. (4) When the Wonsan riot was at its most urgent, overseas Chinese also rushed to the station. The station did not issue tickets specifically to the Chinese, and the same was true for ships. Then their intention to put the Chinese to death is beyond doubt. (5) The strangest thing is that at this time, the telegraph of our country and the telegrams from overseas Chinese to our country, although accepted by the country's telegraph bureau, were all shelved and not sent. The telephone of Chinese businessmen was also not connected. It seems that this suppression of news is helping the evil doers. Although the Japanese people want to embellish with sweet words, how can they hide the facts? According to the above, the Japanese military and police, although claiming to provide protection on the surface, actually intended to indulge in private. It has been found that in the Korean riots in 1927, the number of overseas Chinese who were beaten, killed, and lost was countless. As a result of the negotiations, the Japanese government admitted to compensation and apology and other conditions, but has not fulfilled them for several years. Now a tragedy has occurred, which is a hundred times worse than before. The Korean people's cruelty and brutality are indeed visible to all, and the Japanese people's obvious desire to use the Korean people's violence to carry out their plan to expel overseas Chinese is an undeniable fact. If we do not actively negotiate and urge them to realize it, then the third and fourth tragedies after this will not be avoided, and I am afraid that they will be even worse. Colleagues feel deeply peeled and flustered. In addition to requesting the government and various ministries, departments, and party departments to find ways to protect them, we also ask them to submit a serious protest to the Japanese authorities and conduct earnest negotiations. If the goals of punishing murderers, compensating, and apologizing are not achieved, we will never stop. Therefore, I hereby respectfully inform all circles and ask for your prompt and united assistance to save tens of thousands of overseas Chinese in Korea from deep waters and scorching fire.

Declaration of the General Assembly

The Anti-Japanese and Overseas Chinese Relief Association issued a declaration stating: "This association confirms that the violent anti-Chinese actions throughout Korea are entirely a manifestation of the Japanese government's active aggression in Manchuria and Mongolia. This is evidenced by the Japanese air force's exercises of defensive warfare in the Dalian area and the Japanese army's readiness along the South Manchurian Railway. Under these severe circumstances, we are deeply saddened by the massacre of our compatriots in Korea. To safeguard the future survival of the Chinese nation, we have unanimously resolved at the general assembly to 'permanently sever economic ties with Japan with a resolute and courageous spirit.' In addition to forming a committee to properly discuss effective measures and petition the Central Party Headquarters to instruct local party headquarters to lead the masses in unified action, we sincerely hope that compatriots throughout the country will rise up together and work together. The survival of the nation depends on this one effort. This declaration is hereby made, hoping for your public awareness."

Establishing a Committee

It was resolved to establish a committee to be responsible for this task, named the "Shanghai All Circles Anti-Japanese and Overseas Chinese Relief Committee." Thirty-nine members were determined: nine from the Party Headquarters, eight from the business community, eight from the labor community, two each from the United Citizens' Association, the Education Association, national products organizations, Chinese taxpayer associations, and overseas Chinese organizations, and one each from the agricultural community, the lawyers' association, women's organizations, and news reporters. The list of candidates has been submitted to the Municipal Party Headquarters for review.

Resolutions on Important Cases

The following important cases were resolved by the General Assembly yesterday: (1) Please allocate a portion of the national salvation fund to be telegraphed to Korean Chinese for relief; (2) Please have the National Government issue a severe protest to the Japanese government, ordering (A) the punishment of the rioters who massacred overseas Chinese, compensation for the victims, and compensation for all losses, (B) a solemn apology to our government and people, (C) a solid guarantee that the same or similar atrocities will never occur again, (D) the punishment of Japanese military and police officers in various places, (E) the prohibition of dual nationality, and (F) the negotiation of a new treaty to protect overseas Chinese and trade; (3) It was resolved to hold a memorial service for the murdered overseas Chinese, and the committee was instructed to handle it; (4) Request the National Government to effectively protect the overseas Chinese in Korea and instruct the Japanese government to stop the riots; (5) Request the National Government to strictly order the governments of the northeastern provinces to stop the illegal actions of the Japanese military and police stationed in China and effectively protect the citizens within the country; (6) Implement economic severance with Japan; the committee was instructed to handle the measures; (7) This case is significant and should not be privately settled by local authorities; (8) All proposals not yet passed were handed over to the committee for handling.

Important Proposals

The following proposals, which were not discussed yesterday due to lack of time, were handed over to the committee: (1) Proposed by the Military Uniform Workers' Union: (A) Petition the Central Government to instruct all national mass organizations to uniformly implement compulsory military training to strengthen national power; (B) The Japanese are increasingly insulting us. The recent Wanbaoshan Incident is even more obvious. Please petition the National Government to instruct the whole country to earnestly resist Japanese goods to warn against tyranny; (2) Proposed by the Embroidery Guild: (A) Please have the diplomatic authorities negotiate with Japan to take full responsibility and compensate for loss of life and property; (B) Resisting serves as a background for Koreans, strict measures should be used; (C) Please request the Navy, together with the Army and Air Force, to dispatch warships, etc., to protect overseas Chinese; (3) Proposed by citizen Weng Guoxun: (A) Proactively, telegraph to the national masses to actively promote physical education, aiming for self-defense, in preparation for resisting with force; (B) Our people should act with conscience and implement non-cooperation, i.e., immediately sever economic ties with Japan, and all those employed by the Japanese should withdraw; (4) Proposed by the Diplomatic Association of the Republic of China to the Netherlands: (A) Telegraph the whole country to publicly hold a memorial service for the tragically victimized overseas Chinese in Korea on a scheduled date from the date of receipt of the telegram; (B) From the date of the memorial service, all circles should wear black armbands to mourn the overseas Chinese in Korea; (C) Organize anti-Japanese economic severance throughout the country.

Telegram from Andong

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and Trade Union: Our compatriots in Korea have been brutally expelled and massacred. Five thousand have fled to Andong and local donations have been collected for emergency relief. Many are trapped in Korea, with empty possessions and exhausted food. The injured and wounded are still awaiting care. Your association should take the lead and quickly launch an urgent relief effort and telegraph the whole country to set a day of mourning. Andong National Diplomatic Association, Wen.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegram

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing yesterday, saying: "To the esteemed Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, the persecution of overseas Chinese in Korea was caused by the Wanbaoshan Incident, which was caused by the Japanese using Korean farmers to achieve their goal of invading the eastern provinces. Therefore, before the aftermath of the Korean riots has completely subsided, the Japanese already have a plan to move Korean farmers to cultivate land. The matter must be thoroughly resolved, which shows the Japanese conspiracy. Our country's diplomatic response should also pay attention to this point, otherwise, if one miscalculates, it will be too late to regret, and the eastern provinces will be permanently trapped in an irrecoverable situation. According to international practice, although two countries' people are allowed to engage in commercial business within each other's borders, agricultural cultivation of one hectare is generally limited to the people of the country, except for countries such as Argentina and Brazil in South America. There has never been a case where foreigners are allowed to concurrently engage in agricultural cultivation in the host country. Although Koreans have historical relations with China, since they are under Japanese control, they are a separate country. How can they uniquely enjoy exceptions and allow the Japanese to exploit them as their vanguard for invasion? Korean farmers' immigration to China is based on Article 3 of the Tumen River Boundary Treaty of the third year of Xuantong. According to the provisions of that article, they are only allowed to continue living in the cultivated areas north of the Tumen River. Thus, the scope of allowable immigration according to the treaty is limited to the old Yanji Prefecture of Jilin. This incident occurred in Changchun, which is not a location stipulated in the treaty, and Korean farmers have no right to rent land for cultivation. Over the years, the Liaoning authorities have been misled by the false name of appeasement and allowed Korean farmers to spread throughout Liaoning and Jilin provinces, and the 'Korean farmers obeying Chinese laws and regulations' layer of the Tumen River Boundary Treaty has long been regarded as worthless, merely adding hundreds of thousands of foreign farmers who do not obey Chinese laws and regulations to Liaoning and Jilin provinces, creating a fire, and those with knowledge have long worried that it would erupt. The Wanbaoshan Incident is just the result of years of neglect that should have been received. The Japanese do not plan to thoroughly resolve the matter, but we should have proactively proposed it long ago. For the present plan, we should only, according to Article 3 of the Tumen River Boundary Treaty, investigate all Korean farmers who have over-cultivated in Liaoning and Jilin provinces, and for those who have cultivated land outside the scope of Yanji, the cultivated land should be recovered by the government at a given price or transferred to local farmers at a prepared price. If the Japanese believe that this right has been acquired for many years, and China has been accommodating in the past and should be tolerant in the future, then a special treaty should be signed with the Japanese: (1) These farmers should be recognized by Japan as having fully obtained Chinese nationality and will no longer be treated with dual nationality as before; (2) Koreans who arrive after the treaty is signed should still be handled in accordance with Article 3 of the Tumen River Boundary Treaty. Another issue of the same importance as the Korean farmers' over-cultivation problem is the Japanese freely setting up police stations in the eastern provinces. The relationship of this incident, the cause of the Wanbaoshan incident, lies in this point. If it were not for the extreme tolerance of the eastern provinces authorities, the Jinan May 3rd Incident would have been re-enacted long ago. The Japanese freely set up police stations in the eastern provinces, divided into two types: one is in the railway affiliated areas, and the other is set up in various counties in the eastern provinces. In the fifth year of the Republic of China, during the Zhengjiatun Incident, according to the report of Counselor Wu of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the National Assembly, among the 50+ counties in Liaoning Province, only six or seven counties did not have Japanese setting up police stations freely. This is an extremely shocking thing. Therefore, when the Zhengjiatun case was resolved, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a note to the Japanese ambassador, stating its denial and requesting a general withdrawal. At that time, the person in charge was the late Minister Wu Jun Zhiyong, and your ministry should still have a case to check. In addition to the police set up in the railway affiliated areas, which should be handled at the same time as the recovery of the administrative rights of the railway affiliated areas, the case of freely setting up police stations in various counties has long been forgotten since it was negotiated once in the fifth year of the Republic of China. Since we are now seeking a thorough resolution, it should be proposed together and strive to achieve the goal of completely abolishing the free establishment of police stations, so as to avoid future troubles. We only pray that you will quickly make arrangements to comfort the expectations of the people. It is truly convenient for the public. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Yuan."

Re-Visiting the Foreign Minister

The Wan Case is Still Under Negotiation in Jilin

Documents Transported to Beijing are for Reference

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting received Polish Chargé d'Affaires Weidengtao at the Foreign Ministry Office at 10:30 yesterday morning, Italian Chargé d'Affaires and Consul-General in Shanghai Qiyano at 11:00, and Turkish Chargé d'Affaires Futpei at 11:30. Page 14

Would be transferred to Beijing for negotiation, and that all negotiation documents had been transported to Beijing. What was the truth? Inland River Steamers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Blocked by Great Floods

Various Shipping Bureaus Are Trying to Dredge

Since the beginning of the rainy season, there has been continuous heavy rain, and the water level has risen greatly in various places in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The small inland river steamers, with their paddle wheels plying back and forth, are bound to damage the embankments. The water police have prohibited them from sailing, so recently the small steamers in Suzhou, Hangzhou, and other places have stopped running. Inland trade and transportation have been blocked. Yesterday, for the sake of meeting the demands of merchants and people in various places, the various shipping bureaus in this port agreed on methods to maintain inland river transportation and take into account flood control. This reporter specially went to various parties to investigate and will record the current status of each route as follows:

Shanghai-Wuxi Route

The Shanghai-Wuxi route passes through many towns. Shanghai has China Merchants, Tongyuan, Ruishengxiang, and other ships sailing, and they distribute goods to various towns every day. Recently, since the floods occurred and the ships stopped running, the inland stores have not received goods and have asked the shipping bureaus to resume service. Now, after investigation by the shipping bureaus, the flood situation on this route is that ships traveling upstream above Bacheng and ships traveling downstream below Kunshan cannot sail. In the Kunshan-Bacheng section, the water is level with the shore, and the farmland is in imminent danger. The shipping bureaus have now discussed a relief method. The Shanghai-Wuxi ships will operate as usual, only to Kunshan and Bacheng. In the Kunshan-Bacheng section, small civilian boats will be dispatched to transship goods and passengers. It is planned to start trial navigation today.

Huzhou Line

There are six shipping bureaus operating on the Shanghai-Huzhou route, divided into early and late shifts. Early shift ships such as Yongshun and Yongan have announced that they have stopped sailing. The location of the heavy floods on this route is in the Lishui to Huzhou section. After continuous heavy rain since the 12th, the river surface and farmland are almost indistinguishable. In recent days, farmers have been rushing to dam the area. The late-night ships on this route have agreed to continue to operate as usual, but to drive slower to avoid interfering with the embankments. If it rains again, it is feared that the night ships will also be forced to stop. Many of the goods shipped from Shanghai to Huzhou and passengers going to Huzhou have changed to traveling to Wuxi and then transferring to Taihu Lake.

Hujia Line

The Shanghai-Pinghu route is the most stable. The smaller ships can still operate during this flood. However, although the larger ships are still sailing, when they arrive in Pinghu, they cannot pass the Li Gong Bridge due to the rising water. Therefore, they can only stop in the outer harbor, and all goods and passengers are transferred by civilian boats. Also, the inland river water on the routes through the villages passed by the Jiaxing ships is the greatest. The villagers along the way strictly prohibit ship navigation. If found, they will throw bricks and stones randomly, so they have not yet sailed.

Changshu Class

Shanghai Changshu class is the best in Shanghai's small wheels, with the best passenger cargo of any route wheels. This time, the inland water increased, and the route wheels first stopped, and the acres along the pond were all in the water. If the sky is clear, it can be withdrawn. Now, Shanghai Changshu wheels still have no hope of resuming the shifts. Each class loses 400 or 500 yuan per day. There are also Shensu Ban and Shanghai Hangzhou Ban wheels, which have not been significantly affected. The wheels are still running, but the cargo and passengers transferred to the inland are less than usual because many of the small folk wheels on the roads have stopped.

Municipal Government Negotiates with the Ministry of Industry on National Products Market Cases Yesterday

Formal Reply Will Be Given After the Meeting

Yesterday, the Municipal Government, for the case of the seizure of the National Products Market and the case of the British patrolman shooting and wounding a Chinese policeman on Haig Road, specifically went to the Ministry of Industry in the morning, led by Secretary-General Yu Hongjun and Assistant Secretary Tang, as representatives of the Municipal Government, to negotiate. The secretary of the Ministry of Industry received them. After Yu stated the purpose, the secretary of the Ministry of Industry said that the closure of the National Products Market was entirely due to the poor equipment of the market and for the sake of the safety of the tourists. Therefore, this move was made, and the tourists are all Chinese, so this move by the Ministry of Industry was actually out of good intentions and did not contain any malice. This point should be forgiven by the Municipal Government. As for the three conditions submitted, such as the compensation part, which is beyond the scope of reason, it seems that it cannot be carried out at the same time. The Ministry of Industry's method of closing the dog racing track at the request of the Chinese is also the same. It seems that there is no discrimination against the Chinese. At this point, Secretary-General Yu replied reasonably that the Ministry of Industry's intervention for the sake of the safety of the Chinese is not without considerable reason, but it is only necessary to stop the entertainment department. It should not be closed and stopped along with its business market. This is the first inappropriate measure. The Ministry of Industry closed the entertainment department due to the incomplete equipment, and should also request the court to execute it. The Ministry of Industry does not rely on the law and goes through the procedures of the court, and this is the second fundamental error. As for taking the closure of the dog racing track by the Ministry of Industry as a ratio, in fact, legally speaking, it cannot prohibit people from accusing, so it cannot be taken as a ratio. However, the Municipal Government guarantees that the compensation part will be within the scope of reason and will not be excessive. It is hoped that the Ministry of Industry can also be responsible for accepting these three articles. As a result of the negotiations, the secretary of the Ministry of Industry verbally expressed acceptance and promised to submit it to the Board of Directors for discussion before giving an administrative reply. Then they talked about the case of the British patrolman shooting and wounding a Chinese policeman on Haig Road. According to the reply of the secretary of the Ministry of Industry, the last police meeting had already discussed it once, and a concrete plan would be decided after the police meeting on Wednesday this week.

Public Associations Request a Temporary Suspension of Weights and Measures Inspections

The Shanghai City Bird's Nest, Aromatic Herb, Fruit, Fresh Pork, Pigment & Sundries, Green Bamboo Shoot, Chicken & Duck, and Dried Tobacco Trade Associations, etc., yesterday each appointed representatives to meet and discuss. Regarding the new system of weights and measures, inspections have already commenced, and old instruments must be destroyed. However, various trades still face obstacles due to the differences between the old and new systems, making it difficult to comply with the limited time for conversion. The difficulties have already been presented to the City Chamber of Commerce, which then forwarded them to the City Social Affairs Bureau for review and a decision on extending the implementation deadline. As a response has not yet been received, why the urgency for inspections? Wouldn't this only create disturbance? It was immediately resolved to submit another petition to the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it forward the situation to the Social Affairs Bureau and request an extension until January 1st of next year for implementation. Separately, a formal letter was submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau, requesting a temporary suspension of inspections. The original text is recorded below:

Presented to earnestly request a postponement of the inspection of new weights and measures equipment, in order to allow time for preparation. The associations, etc., received an order to promote the new system of weights and measures, and immediately notified all member firms to comply. However, those who have adopted the new system are still few in number. Furthermore, the new and old instruments differ in their systems. This year and last year, the old system was still used. To suddenly make a change at this time, with goods entering and leaving throughout the year, and the measurement methods differing at the beginning and end, would cause great inconvenience in accounting and settlement. This type of difficulty has already been reported to your bureau through the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting an extension of the inspection deadline. Whether this is feasible is currently awaiting your instructions and decision. Recently, it was reported that your bureau and the Public Security Bureau jointly issued a notice, stating that inspections would begin on the 11th of this month. However, many businesses have not yet had time to prepare, and manufacturers are struggling to keep up with the numerous orders. It is difficult to enforce a uniform adoption at the same time. A sudden inspection would only waste effort and may even cause further disturbances. In addition to sending another letter to the City Chamber of Commerce to report the situation again, we fear that the official documents will take days to transmit. Therefore, we are submitting this joint petition in advance, explaining the difficulties in complying with the deadline to adopt the new system of weights and measures, and sending representatives to present our request. We earnestly beseech your bureau to consider the merchants' difficulties, and approve forwarding this to the Public Security Bureau, to temporarily suspend the execution of inspections, so that businesses can prepare for the change and avoid disputes. This would truly be for the public good, etc.

Department Store Association Telegrams Beijing Requesting Reduction in Business Tax

The Department Store Trade Association yesterday sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, stating:

"Respectfully to Your Excellency, Ministry of Finance. Upon investigation of the Shanghai City business tax rate schedule, the department store industry is listed at three per mille. Our association believes that the tax rate is too high and the business sector cannot bear the burden. Representatives were sent to Beijing to petition and personally delivered a request for a reduction. We were grateful that Your Ministry considered this, and on the 10th of this month, the Shanghai City Finance Bureau Business Tax Preparatory Office sent a formal letter No. 1, 2, and 3 to the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, stating, 'Upon investigation, the department store tax rate has already been submitted to the Finance Bureau, which has forwarded it to the City Government to consult with the Ministry of Finance for review. The request to merge into the Beijing-Guangdong foreign goods industry for taxation should be processed after receiving the Ministry of Finance's approval.' The letter was approved as previously stated. It is appropriate to reply to your association for your information,' etc. Upon investigation, the nature of the department store industry is the same as the foreign goods industry. As stated in the June 2nd newspaper, Your Ministry sent a consultation letter No. 1946 to the Hubei Provincial Government regarding the term 'fu,' which explains the business tax regulations, regarding whether department stores in major commercial ports should be considered part of the foreign goods industry and should be clearly defined. According to the nature of department stores, they are essentially an expansion of the Beijing-Guangdong foreign goods business. Therefore, business tax should be temporarily collected according to the Beijing-Guangdong foreign goods industry,' etc. Now, in the Shanghai draft, the tax collection for the foreign goods industry is two per mille, which is already considered high. However, the tax on the department store industry is actually three per mille. This not only contradicts the meaning of Your Ministry's explanation but also does not align with commercial realities. Therefore, we urgently present this statement, requesting a swift correction, so that the department store business tax in Shanghai City does not exceed two per mille, which is deeply appreciated by the public. The Shanghai City Department Store Trade Association bows."

Silk Industry Public Bond Fundamental Solution Approved

Jiangzhe Silk Reeling Machine Registration Procedures Completed

The Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bond Executive Committee held its seventh meeting yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM at the Commodity Inspection Bureau. The committee members Mu Qichu, Zou Bingwen, Chen Shutang, Chu Jianzeng, Shen Huachen, Qian Fenghao, and expert committee members Zhou Tingding, Zheng Bijang, etc., eight people in total, were present. Mu Qichu chaired the meeting. As a result of the discussion:

(1) The request to exempt silk reeling from taxes was resolved to be difficult to implement.

(2) The method of levying a special tax on double cocoon silk was resolved to be presented to the Ministry of Industry to order the customs to collect the tax uniformly from the date of receiving the Ministry's order. For those that have not been collected before, the Commodity Inspection Bureau will be ordered to investigate and make up the payment and transfer it to the Fund Management Committee.

(3) The fundamental solution was approved according to the amended plan. The amended regulations for installing machinery and blackboards are recorded below:

(1) Each manufacturer must register within the time period stipulated by the Executive Committee. After registration, they must install the equipment within the time period stipulated by the Executive Committee. After the installation is completed, the subsidy can be paid out only after the Executive Committee has inspected it.

(2) If a manufacturer is unwilling to report the installation within the time period, they will be allowed to report the installation within two months after the expiration date. If they still do not report the installation after the expiration date, the payment of their subsidy will be suspended.

Furthermore, the silk reeling machine registration procedures in Jiangzhe have been completed. The statistics are as follows: 26,066 units in Shanghai, 1,593 double cocoon units, 14,438 units in Wuxi, and 7,732 units in Zhejiang, totaling 49,829 units. The committee will submit a document to the Ministry for review in the coming days.

Dr. Love's Work After Coming to China

Dr. Love, the American agricultural higher adviser of the Ministry of Industry and the chief technician for crop improvement in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, came to China in April of this year. After his arrival, he went to Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to inspect the work of various agricultural experimental fields. He is currently studying the current system and experimental methods of each field based on the results of the inspection to see if there are any changes and improvements that should be made so that he can contribute to the authorities. During the inspection, Dr. Love and Dr. Shen Zonghan, a technician at the Zhejiang Agriculture and Forestry General Station, selected many excellent single spikes of wheat in preparation for planting this winter to conduct comparative experiments next year to gradually cultivate excellent varieties so that farmers can obtain more harvest using the same cultivation methods. In addition to the inspection, Dr. Love plans to convene technicians from various experimental fields and agricultural schools in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces this winter to conduct several months of training. This month, he also contacted Jinling University to organize a crop discussion meeting and give lectures on crop statistical methods to increase the knowledge of the listeners about agricultural experimental methods. It is reported that as many as 79 agricultural affairs agencies from various provinces went to Ningbo to participate in the discussion meeting.

Swindled Out of a Large Sum After Being Kidnapped

Still Not Out of Danger After Being Kidnapped for Over a Year

Swindled Out of a Large Sum by Someone Entrusted to Help

Two Relatives of the Defendant Deny Fraud

Lin Zengrong, son of Lin Jiang of No. 69 Rue Poussin, French Concession, was kidnapped by bandits in February of last year and has not yet been rescued for more than a year. The police have now found that after the case occurred, Fang Daoquan, Jing Bodil, Jing Guangfu, etc., went to the victim's home on the pretext of helping to negotiate with the bandits in an attempt to swindle a large sum of money. Fang and others were arrested, and they were brought to the French Court yesterday for questioning. First, the Western detective explained the background of the case. Then, the plaintiff, Lin Jiang, stated that after her son was kidnapped, the woman entrusted Zhang Jiaping to negotiate with the bandits and was successively swindled out of 18,000 yuan, but her son was still not rescued. Therefore, she entrusted relatives Jing Bodil and his son Jing Guangfu and Fang Daoquan to help find a solution, but they still had no success and fabricated her son's handwritten letter and fake telegrams, etc., in an attempt to defraud her. However, my son was kidnapped and has not yet been rescued, and his whereabouts are unknown. My husband died of grief because of this. I am seeking justice. The defendants, Jing Bodil and Jing Guangfu, father and son, hired lawyers Plamée and Fessenden to defend them, claiming that Jing Bodil is the father-in-law of the kidnapped person Lin Zengrong, and Jing Guangfu is the brother-in-law of the kidnapped person. After Lin was kidnapped last year, he entrusted the defendants, father and son, to find a way to rescue him. The defendants, father and son, then entrusted Fang Daoquan to assist in the handling. The plaintiff's side entrusted a person surnamed Shen to send 7,500 yuan to the defendants, etc. Later, the money was returned in full, which shows that although the defendants helped to handle the matter, they did not commit any fraud. When the plaintiff was at the police station, the captain asked her why she wanted to sue the defendants, and the plaintiff replied that a sage (that is, a witch) told her that if she wanted her son to be rescued, she must investigate the closest relatives, so she filed a lawsuit. It can be seen that the plaintiff completely misunderstood the slander of the witch and filed the lawsuit. We are seeking a clear investigation. The officer asked Fang Daoquan, why did you want to fabricate telegrams to deceive the plaintiff? Fang replied that it was because Jing Guangfu told me that because his sister had fainted several times since his brother-in-law Lin Zengrong was kidnapped, in order to protect his sister's life, he forged the telegram from Zhenjiang asking about the delivery of goods and pretended it was a telegram from the kidnappers, falsely claiming that if 7,500 yuan could be paid, they would release him, etc., to reassure her. There was no act of fraud. The witness Lin Jing said that after her husband was kidnapped, she first entrusted Zhang Jiaping to negotiate with the bandits and was swindled out of 18,000 yuan, but there were still no results. Therefore, the woman asked her father and brother to help with the handling, which is true. The Chinese and Western officials adjourned to wait for the verdict.

A Fisherman's Drifting Record

Xu Zhitang Makes a Living by Catching Cuttlefish

A Small Boat Meets a Hurricane at the Foot of the Mountain

Experiences Two Days and Nights of Terrifying Waves

Fortunately, Met a Japanese Ship and Was Rescued Alive

Around 4:00 PM on the day before yesterday (the 12th), the Japanese trading company Mitsui & Co.'s ship Munakata Maru, was sailing from Japan to Ma'anshan outside Wusongkou. While passing through the waters of Daji Mountain, the ship's owner, Japanese J. Kawazoe, was in the pilothouse, using binoculars to observe the route. He unintentionally saw something like a small boat in the distance, floating with the waves, and saw someone lying down in the small boat. Therefore, he was very surprised and ordered the ship to follow the small boat. When they got close, they saw someone in the small boat. They then ordered the sailors to lower the lifeboat and sail to check. They saw the person in the small boat lying motionless and barely breathing. They devised a method to drag the person and the small boat onto the ship. The ship's doctor performed emergency surgery, and the person gradually woke up. The ship owner and others asked him why he was drifting in the ocean. He said his name was Xu Zhitang, from Jiangshan, Ningbo. He was thirty-four years old and made a living by catching cuttlefish. He lived in Wangjiajingting Township, Jiangshan, and had a wife and two sons at home. On the morning of the 11th, he was catching cuttlefish alone in a small boat near Qushan. When he returned to the foot of Xianaoshan, a hurricane suddenly blew up, and the small boat could not control itself and drifted with the wind. Xu hurriedly used all his strength to row the boat to the shore, but unexpectedly, the waves were like mountains and seas and pushed the small boat out to sea, further away from the shore. Xu had exhausted his strength and had no way to escape. Knowing that there was no hope of survival, he used a rope to tie himself and the boat tightly together and had to let it drift with the waves. After drifting in the ocean for a day and night, he was soaked by strong winds and heavy rain. Xu was hungry and cold and soon lost consciousness. The small boat drifted in the ocean for another day until it was rescued by a Japanese ship before he woke up, etc. The ship's owner and others took pity on his situation and provided food and courteous treatment. When the ship returned to Shanghai from Ma'anshan and sailed into Wusongkou at around 7:00 AM yesterday, Chen Shoujing, the inspector of the Wusong branch office of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Foreigner Passport Inspection Office, boarded the ship for inspection. The Japanese ship owner told him the story. Inspector Chen Shoujing then took Xu Zhitang and the small boat to Wusong and sent them to the Songsi Fourth Detachment of the Water Patrol Team. After Captain Xiao Ping questioned him, Xu recounted the story, and Captain Ding sent a quick letter to his family on his behalf and sent the police to escort Xu to the Water Patrol Headquarters in Nanshi for disposition.

Dispute Over a Concubine Contract

Zhang Deqing Sued by Concubine for Breach of Contract

Defendant's Lawyer Claims No Written Agreement Exists

Zhang Deqing, a shareholder and manager of the Guizhou Road China Hotel and a native of Huzhou who also owns the New World Hotel in Wuxi, is currently forty-six years old. In June of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, he took a woman named Zhang Wanshi as his concubine in Wuxi. The woman was from Wuxi and was thirty-two years old. At the time, both parties signed a contract containing four conditions: (1) Zhang would provide the woman with a monthly living allowance of sixty yuan; (2) Zhang would allocate a portion of his property to Wanshi as a means of support in her old age; (3) Zhang would not take any further concubines; and (4) If he were to break the agreement, he would be subject to legal sanctions. However, since they began living together, Zhang has not fulfilled the agreement. Recently, he even took a woman named Mei Mei as a concubine and spent thousands of taels of silver on clothing and jewelry for her. Upon hearing this news, Wanshi immediately traveled to Shanghai to confront Zhang at the China Hotel. However, Zhang refused to meet with her. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Yi of the Tenth Civil Court summoned the defendant Zhang Deqing, who did not appear. Instead, lawyer Ye Shaoying appeared on his behalf. First, lawyer Zhang, representing the plaintiff, stated the grounds for the lawsuit and presented the contract as evidence. Less than three months after the defendant and the plaintiff began their relationship, the plaintiff's husband found out and accused the defendant of adultery and fleeing. This was reported in the Wuxi newspapers at the time. Later, an out-of-court settlement was reached, and the plaintiff and the defendant separated. However, no written agreement was made. Now, the plaintiff has suddenly filed a lawsuit with this court, which is quite extraordinary. He then presented the Wuxi newspapers as evidence. Judge Yang stated that the case needed to be investigated by the Wuxi County Government and ordered both parties to withdraw and await a rescheduled hearing.

Dredging of the South Shanghai Wharf

Commences Today

Since the Shanghai South Steamboat Wharf was taken over by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, it has been recognized that the wharf's shore is silted up and shallow, making it difficult for steamboats to dock, which has greatly affected the market in South Shanghai. It was reported to Mayor Zhang, who consulted with Director Song of the Whangpoo Conservancy Bureau. It was decided that the Bureau would undertake the dredging project, which will begin today at Wharf No. 1, Dongmen Road, 16 Pu, and continue to Dongjiadu. The entire project is expected to take about four months to complete. During the construction, an area of 1,000 feet in front and behind the dredger must be kept clear. The Bureau of Public Works has sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, instructing the water patrol to temporarily prohibit all ships from navigating or docking within this area to avoid obstructing the construction. It is also understood that the Bureau of Public Works plans to take advantage of the opportunity to dismantle and repair the floating docks, as the dredging of one wharf shore will render four docks unusable at the same time. It is reported that the Bureau of Public Works has requested the Bureau of Engineering to promptly invite merchants to estimate the cost of the repairs so that they can be carried out simultaneously.

Garrison Command Executes Culprits in Wang Baoxiang Murder Case

Zhu Shoutong and Zhou Xinsheng Sentenced to Death

Qiu Changgao Sentenced to Two Years of Imprisonment

Zhou Xisan and Others Vigorously Pursued and Brought to Justice

The Far East News Agency reports that Wang Baoxiang, a native of Funing, Jiangsu, has lived in Shanghai for over forty years and founded many charitable organizations. He was particularly active in revolutionary work, providing assistance to revolutionary party members in Shanghai who were in difficulty. He sacrificed his family's wealth and resources, and everyone considered him to have a chivalrous spirit. During the Northern Expedition of the Party Army in the sixteenth year of the Republic, Wang personally led revolutionary comrades in response. After the military was settled, Commander Gu Zhutong appointed him as a senior advisor to reward his revolutionary contributions. In the winter of that year, he returned to his hometown on business. When the ship reached the Yushan River, he was unexpectedly murdered by Zhu Shoutong and Zhou Xisan, who had been his followers for many years and were related to him, in collusion with Zhou Xinsheng, Qiu Changgao, Wang Xinliang, Wang Er, Qiu Changlin, and others. He was shot three times and died immediately. His body was abandoned in the river by Qiu Changgao. Later, his family discovered it and reported it to the Funing County Government, which arrested Zhu Shoutong and others. After being informed that the case involved military affairs and should be punished according to military law, they were presented to the Military and Political Department of Tian, which designated the Songhu Garrison Command to hear the case. It is reported that the Military Law Office conducted multiple interrogations and sentenced the criminals. Zhu Shoutong and Zhou Xinsheng were sentenced to death for their roles in robbery and murder. The sentence was approved by the Military and Political Department and carried out by firing squad yesterday. Qiu Changgao was sentenced to two years of imprisonment and four years of deprivation of public rights for abandoning the body. The remaining fugitive accomplices Zhou Xisan, Wang Xinliang, Wang Er, and Qiu Changlin are all wanted and will be brought to justice to uphold justice. Wang's relatives and friends, upon hearing the news of the execution of the murderers, were all grateful for the fairness and impartiality of the law enforcers.

A Lifetime of Love, One Death, One Survival

Man Ma Shouxiang is Dead

Woman Ma Alan is Well

At 1:20 PM on the 12th, the Huis police station at the North Railway Station, No. 5 Jielu Road, reported that a male and female guest in Room 11 of the North Railway Station Hotel had attempted suicide by taking poison due to passionate love. The man was speechless, and the woman was still alive. The police officer inquired about the date of arrival, names, and occupations of the male and female guests. It was reported that the guests arrived at the hotel at 4:00 PM on the 11th. The male guest claimed to be Dong Chenxue, 22 years old, a silk merchant from Wuxi. The woman's name was Ma Alan, also 22 years old, from Wuxi. The male and female guests were seen entering and leaving together, very intimate, and whispering sweet nothings. There was no sign of suicide. Today, when the waiter saw that the guests had not opened the door, he had to inquire whether the room needed to be renewed according to the rules. However, after knocking on the door for a long time, there was no response. Knowing that something was wrong, he managed to pry open the door and found an empty opium paste box on the table, indicating that they had taken poison. The police officer dispatched detectives to the hotel to investigate and found a suicide note on the pillow, which stated, "We two will end our lives here, but we do not want anyone to know after death. We only wish to be buried together." The man and woman were immediately taken to Guangren Hospital for treatment. However, the man had taken too much poison and died shortly after arriving at the hospital. His body was taken to the forensic examination center on Fielun Road for examination. Yesterday, the female guest, Ma Alan, recovered and was sent back to the police station. After further questioning by the police officer, she stated that the deceased's real name was Ma Shouxiang, a painter in Wuxi, with a wife and a three-year-old daughter. He had fallen in love with her a long time ago. Later, she married someone else, but her husband died not long after. Ma Shouxiang then asked her to rekindle their love, but she refused, as several people were flirting with her at the time. Ma Shouxiang eventually became ill from unrequited love. She pitied his sincerity and agreed to his request. Ma recovered from his illness. Today's double suicide was due to economic pressure and family disapproval. They did not want to live alone, so they asked to be buried together. It is reported that the case will be taken to court for trial today.

Two Thousand Yuan Savings Passbook Suddenly Becomes a Fake

Passbook Hidden in Chest

Wife Took it Out to Mortgage

Afraid of Husband's Discovery

Created a Fake Passbook to Conceal

Tang Guitao, 59 years old, from Songjiang, has been running a Jiangcao shop at No. 51 Wangjiazuijiao, Xiaonanmenwai, in the South City. His business is thriving. Tang had deposited two thousand yuan in foreign currency at the Detai Xing Doumai Bank. The passbook was hidden in a chest. The other day, due to an urgent need, he opened the chest and took the passbook to the bank to withdraw the funds. However, the bank carefully examined it and recognized that the passbook was not issued by the bank, and the seal on the passbook was also a counterfeit. Tang was greatly shocked upon hearing this and immediately rushed home. Because the chest was managed by his wife, he repeatedly questioned his wife about the whereabouts of the passbook and the origin of the fake passbook. Tang's wife was forced to confess that last year a neighbor, Chen Ren, borrowed silver from her due to an urgent need. Because she lacked cash, she gave the passbook from the chest to Chen Ren to mortgage it somewhere. She was afraid that you would find out about this matter and blame her, so she asked Chen Ren to forge a passbook and put it back in the chest. Tang was extremely angry upon hearing this and immediately went to Chen Ren's house and summoned Zhang Chunren, the guard at the Ninth Post, to bring her back to the First Branch of the First District. During the preliminary interrogation, the head of the station, Tang, recounted the previous events and requested a thorough investigation. Chen Ren confessed that she was 38 years old, a native of Nanjing, and had been running the Chen Hongxing Pen Shop at No. 53 Wangjiazuijiao. On February 12th of last year, she borrowed 1,200 yuan from Tang's wife due to an urgent need. Later, she borrowed another 700 yuan, for a total of 1,900 yuan, and it was agreed that the monthly interest rate would be 3%, so she had to pay 57 yuan in interest every month, which she had never interrupted. Recently, business in the store has been poor, so she has been two months in arrears. As for the fake passbook, she did not forge it. However, she had seen Tang's wife give a blank passbook to her shop assistant Zhou Dingxiang to fill out. But she did not know what he wrote. The police then summoned Zhou to the case for questioning. He confessed that he was 32 years old, a native of Chongming. In February of last year, Tang's wife brought a blank passbook and asked him to fill in the words "Deposit 2,000 yuan in foreign currency" on the passbook. He did not agree at first, but Tang's wife claimed that it did not matter. He could not refuse her request, so he wrote it on her behalf. However, he did not know about the fake seal on the passbook. Considering the complexity of the case and its importance, they were ordered to be detained separately pending investigation.

The Li Guojun's Daughter, Li Jiazhen, Lawsuit Concludes

Judgment Scheduled for the 18th

Li Jiazhen, the daughter of Li Guojun, was betrothed to Zhang Jinjiang from a young age. At that time, she was young and ignorant and did not object. As she grew older, she realized that the Zhang family was gradually declining and feared that she would face difficulties in the future. She expressed her opposition to her father, who agreed to provide her with a dowry of 22,000 yuan, with 8,000 yuan for wedding attire and 12,000 yuan deposited in a bank to generate interest for her daily living expenses. However, in 1929, her father passed away. On his deathbed, he made an oral will stating that 100 yuan should be given to Jiazhen each month for her daily use with her husband. Later, Jiazhen and her husband had a falling out and she left him, filing a lawsuit with the Special District Court demanding that her stepmother hand over the 12,000 yuan. This case has been reported in this newspaper several times, and the court has also held several hearings. Yesterday was the last hearing. Neither the plaintiff nor the defendant appeared. The plaintiff's attorney stated that the case was originally intended to be settled out of court, but the defendant showed no sincerity, which led to the breakdown of the settlement. The plaintiff is currently in the hospital due to illness and is in great need of funds for all expenses. Moreover, Guojun and his brother Mugong jointly own 3 million taels of family property, which has not been divided. This small amount is easy to raise. As for the 3 million in inheritance, a lawsuit has also been filed based on the law that women have inheritance rights. As for the defendant's claim that there is a will that can prove it, her father was already in a coma when he was dying and only made an oral will, without a written will. This was something the plaintiff witnessed personally at the time. Now, a written will has suddenly been discovered, which the plaintiff completely denies. The defendant's lawyer then presented the will to the court and claimed that when Li Guojun was in critical condition, he asked this lawyer to go and verify it. Because he had to go to Hangzhou, he entrusted assistant lawyer Xu Enjing to act on his behalf and affix a seal. Therefore, the plaintiff's claim that there is no such will is untrue. As for the 3 million in family property, there has not yet been a detailed accounting. It is still difficult to determine whether there is a surplus or a deficit. Moreover, most of the real estate is located in the original home in Hefei. Currently, bandits are rampant everywhere, and even if the amount is as claimed by the plaintiff, it would not be convenient to go there to sell it. Therefore, only 100 yuan can be given each month to meet Jiazhen's daily needs. He requested that the court reject the plaintiff's lawsuit. The court ordered the debate to begin. After the plaintiff's and defendant's lawyers finished their arguments, the court scheduled a judgment for the 18th.

Six Bandits Each Imprisoned for Five Years in Western Prison

Bandits Shi Ludao, Yang A Si, Cai Jinsheng, Zhu Ruilin, Hu Ruisheng, and Lin A Er, etc., on the evening of the 25th of last month, at 2:00 a.m., intercepted a woman on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession and stole a money bag and a platinum watch from her and fled. Jin Jiulin, special investigator of the French Police Department, detective Li Yaolong, deputy detective Qian Yumin, Mao Jinggen, Zhang Ziying, etc., investigated and apprehended Shi and the six bandits together, confiscated a pistol from Yang A Si, and recovered the stolen goods. Wang Chen Shi was also brought into the police station by the woman. Yesterday, they were taken to the French Public Concession for interrogation. First, the head of the Western Investigation team reported the previous events. The defendants confessed to the robbery. Wang Chen Shi said that the woman had been in a relationship with Zhu Ruilin for a short time and did not know about the theft. She asked for mercy. Chinese and Western officials sentenced Yang A Si and Cai Jinsheng to five years in the Western prison, and then they were deported and sent to the mainland for trial. Shi Jin Dao, Hu Ruisheng, Zhu Ruilin, and Lin A Er were each imprisoned for five years, and after their release, they were permanently deported from the Concession. The pistol was confiscated, and Wang Chen Shi was deported.

Yu Tai Oil and Rice Store Theft Case Solved

Three Bandits Taken to the Bureau for Interrogation

The Yu Tai Oil and Rice Store at No. 1, Lane 22, Xiaoyangjia House, Pudong, was robbed by several bandits on the evening of the 6th of this month, with a loss of about 400 yuan. The owner, Shen Shaoyun, reported the case to the Fourth Police Team, which in turn reported it to the Third District and submitted it to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. The other day, Third District detectives Zhang Yong and Yang Jinsen apprehended the bandit Gu Futang (aka Tao Tao). Under strict interrogation, Gu confessed that he was 26 years old, a native of Pudong, living near No. 30,000 Changjia House, doing small business. He admitted to having robbed the Yu Tai Oil and Rice Store with accomplices Xu Zhangquan, Xi Aqiu, Xiao Chongming, etc. The stolen goods were divided in Room 19 of the Suzhou Hotel, and he received 15 yuan in silver and 13,000 copper coins. He was ordered to be detained. At the same time, detectives were sent to apprehend the escaped bandits. Unexpectedly, Gu, fearing punishment, suddenly attempted to hang himself with his belt in the detention center. Police Captain Zhang discovered this and cut the belt down. Fortunately, it was not long before he lost consciousness. He was taken out of the detention center, given a small amount of Sha Yao water for his stomach cramps, and placed under strict guard. Xu Zhangquan and Xi Aqiu were soon apprehended by the original detectives. Xu claimed to be 20 years old, a local, living at No. 8 Tongxing Street, working at the Xiang Sheng Iron Factory. Xi claimed to be 20 years old, a native of Nanhui, living on Banbian Street, Sanwanchang, running a tofu shop. Both denied being bandits and claimed that Gu Futang had framed them out of hatred. They requested an investigation. The district head, considering the case involved robbery, did not dare to decide on his own and ordered Gu, Xu, and Xi, along with the informant Shen Xiaodi, to be taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation yesterday afternoon.

Jingguang Optical Company Stolen a Large Amount of Valuable Goods

Showroom Located on Main Thoroughfare

Thieves Highly Skilled

The Shanghai Times reports that the goods displayed in the showroom of the Jingguang Optical Company at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Henan Road were stolen clean by thieves after midnight on Saturday. According to its managing director, Lei Guxun, the total value is estimated to be several thousand taels of silver. The showroom is located on a main thoroughfare, with a constant stream of pedestrians day and night, and the streetlights shine brightly both inside and out. However, thieves were able to enter and take everything without anyone noticing, leaving the detectives handling the case in doubt. Moreover, patrol officers are stationed near the company day and night. However, neither before nor after the incident were any suspicious people seen loitering nearby. Even the patrolling officers who passed by the company's windows that night did not see anything unusual inside. The first person to discover the theft was Lei Guxun. According to his report to the police station, he was walking along Nanjing Road at around 3:00 a.m. when he stopped and looked back at the company. He saw that the lights in the showroom were bright and the items were in disarray. The display cabinets had been pried open, and the valuables had been taken clean. He immediately reported it to the police station. As of late Sunday night, the detectives' investigation had not yielded any clues.
