Incoming Letters

Sir, On the 13th of this month, in the local news section of your newspaper, you published a message that the Municipal Public Security Bureau intends to inspect the bodies of foreigners coming to China. After investigation, our bureau has not yet made such a proposal, nor has it received any orders regarding this matter. I urgently request that you make a correction to conform to the facts. Sincerely, Chief Editor, Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, Secretariat, July 13th.

Sir, I have read the news in your newspaper on July 12th about the suspension of Shanghai-Manchuria airmail and the delivery by train. The facts are not true and may be a misrepresentation of rumors. After investigation, the Shanghai-Manchuria air route of our company was affected by adverse weather conditions a few days ago, and Flight No. 2 landed in Outer Mongolia, causing a misunderstanding. Furthermore, the continuous plum rains in the north and south caused trains and ships in various places to stop. Our company also temporarily suspended two flights. Later, in view of the importance of postal transportation, which cannot be stagnated, it was decided that the flight schedule would be temporarily changed to one round trip each week to the north and south starting from the 12th of this month, that is, from Shanghai to Manchuria every Sunday, and from Manchuria to Shanghai every Tuesday (all departure and arrival times are in accordance with the original schedule and will not be changed), and airmail will be transported as usual to avoid suspension of postal services. Once the misunderstanding of the Outer Mongolia incident is explained, the weather improves, and there are no more obstacles, the flight will still be operated according to the original schedule. The company has notified the newspapers on the 12th and published an important notice declaring the change of schedule, and there is no suspension of flights or delivery of mail by train. In order to prevent people from not knowing the truth, I hereby request that you check and make corrections, which will be greatly appreciated. Sincerely, Shenbao, Eurasia Airlines, July 13th.

Page 17

Free Talk

World Anecdotes

— Sea Guest

School on the Train

The government of Canada pays extraordinary attention to children's education. They believe that if children cannot go to school, then the school should accommodate them and move the teaching to them. With this principle in mind, they resolutely implemented it. In several places in Ontario Province, most of the people make a living by logging. They travel with their families to log, and it is impossible for them to live in one place for a long time. Therefore, their children cannot be enrolled in ordinary schools. The education authorities came up with a novel idea to use trains as schools. The trains were equipped with desks and seats, like classrooms, and traveled back and forth on the 600-mile-long railway, gathering children along the way to study. Although the area is vast and the time is limited, each child cannot go to school every day, but they still receive some considerable education.

The Cleanest City in the World

In any country or metropolis in the world, it is inevitable to see untidy streets and public places. Although the municipal authorities are very strict about garbage disposal, there are still many people who like to discard discarded tram tickets, bus tickets, cigarette butts, and empty cigarette cases. Even the authorities in London have repeatedly considered banning it, but ultimately nothing can be done. But there is one place in the world that can actually do this, and that is Sydney, New South Wales, Australia. First, the local authorities announced to the whole city that anyone who pollutes the streets from a certain day in a certain month by discarding a tram ticket on the street will be arrested and fined without exception. From then on, the citizens unconsciously became clean, and Sydney became the cleanest city in the world.

A Record of the Tomb of Hongfu in Liling, Hunan

— Heavenly Hatred

I enjoy listening to people talk about historical sites. Whenever someone treats me to stories of famous historical sites, I cannot help but lean forward and forget my fatigue. Whenever I meet good friends in different places, I always bother them to talk about the historical sites of their hometowns for my own pleasure. Over a lifetime, I have heard countless stories. Unfortunately, I am a hard-working person with no ability to travel extensively, so I have heard a hundred times but seen nothing, only indulging in dreams. Recently, I met a friend from Hunan who told me that few people know where Hongfu, the beauty of the Sui Dynasty, is buried. Now I will tell you that her tomb is located at the foot of Xishan, across the river in Liling County, Hunan. Even the people of Hunan did not know about it seven or eight years ago. It was lost in the weeds. Fortunately, the broken stele was still there, not completely erased. When Zhao Hengti was in charge of Hunan, Ye Qi's brigade, part of Liu Xing's Second Division, was stationed there. A staff officer named He in the brigade headquarters was an elegant scholar. One day, he wandered to Xishan and saw a broken stele lying on the ground. He rubbed the inscriptions and recognized it as the place where Hongfu was buried. So he joined with local gentry to donate money for repairs. Once completed, a tall stele was erected in front of the tomb, inscribed with "The Tomb of Hongfu." A pavilion was built next to the tomb. Mr. He wrote a couplet himself: "Hongfu would know me if she knew; How fortunate this green mountain is to bury fragrance." He also widened the steep and sloping road in front of the tomb and planted peach and willow trees on both sides for decoration. Since then, it has become a place for travelers to visit. Hongfu's name has suddenly become well-known among the people of Liling, no less than Zhenniang of Wu and Kuai and Su Xiaoxiao of Qiantang. Although the green mountain is fortunate, it is also fortunate for Hongfu. If she knows in the underworld, she should be grateful to staff officer He. According to my research, Hongfu was originally a courtesan of Yang Su, the prime minister of the Sui Dynasty. Her surname was Zhang and her name was Chuchen. When Li Jing visited Su in plain clothes, the concubines were lined up. Among them, there was a woman holding a red whisk. She had a special beauty and stared at Jing alone. That night, Jing returned to his inn, and Hongfu ran to him, saying, "I am Hongfu, a courtesan of the Yang family. I am willing to entrust myself to a tall tree." Then she went with him to Taiyuan. As for why her tomb is in Liling, my friend said that it is said among the people of Hunan that Hongfu followed Li Jing on an expedition and died of illness while stationed in Liling. So she was buried at the foot of Xishan. The truth is impossible to verify. However, Zhenniang and Su Xiao are also impossible to verify. Even the tomb of the Fragrant Concubine of the Qing Dynasty, which is less than two hundred years old, has been disputed and it is impossible to determine which is true and which is false. Moreover, why should we insist on such a rigid view of Hongfu?

Responding to Mr. Hu Zhentang's "Three Hundred Chu Saws Without Emulating the Original Rhyme" in One Verse

— Yuan Xiluo

Human art is often not as good as heavenly masters. A clever hand writes an article as casually as poetry. When the butterfly dream awakens, Zhou is also an illusion. When the grub swallows, Zhong is also foolish. The wind and clouds tattoo the eyes for three thousand eons. The stars embroider the chest for twelve hours. When the book city is eaten by bookworms, only one sentence remains. Boldly claim that the bamboo slips are in the heart.

Four Poems Presented to Mr. Yu Qiaqing on the 50th Anniversary of His Stay in Shanghai

— Tao Zaidong

I also schemed to go south for five years, turning the numbers upside down as if they were from heaven. It can be known that those who achieve fame in the world are destined to have longevity.

The robbery of the White Gate was a miracle for a hundred years. The Yellow Peril just startled the sleeping lion. It is just around the corner to create a new Shanghai. Fight with you to the end of your life.

Neither an official nor a hermit, also not a merchant. Neither rich nor poor, nor a crowned king. I would like to create a glorious model with my countrymen. I give you a first-class certificate of freedom. (Giving freedom is considered a grand event in Europe. Prime Minister Yingmai received this honor last summer.)

The Three Northern Regions are managed as an autonomous region. The hard work of many years has been a good plan. At the Golden Embankment, I listen to the wind and waves at night. My humble official's footprints are recorded in the sea corner.

A Small Record of the New Green Lotus Pavilion

— Wang Yanjin

The three characters "Green Lotus Pavilion" are known to almost every woman and child in Shanghai. Since moving to the opposite side of the Immortal World, it has been renovated and its appearance has been completely renewed. The elegance of today is far from comparable to the humility of the past. Yesterday was the anniversary of its completion, and manager Sun Shaorui invited the press to declare the reform of the nature of Biaolian Pavilion, so that poets and writers would know where to go.

The Past and Present in the Mouth of the Owner Mr. Sun briefly said that when the Green Lotus Pavilion was first established on Fourth Road, it was a place for the lower classes to play. Countless young workers fell into depravity here. I am really to blame. So I planned a reform plan, but I was trapped by the environment and it was difficult to realize it for a while. Now that this new house is completed, it is moved here. The business nature is different from before, and the equipment is also different. The second floor is a general bookstore and a place for various industries to sell and negotiate. The third floor has a special elegant seat, which is specially for poets and writers to discuss papers.

The Disappointment of the Daily Reporter Two reporters from Shanghai Daily News, Tiichiro and Sugato Harutei, were also present on time that evening. The two reporters thought that they would be able to eat Chinese food here today. Unexpectedly, Mr. Sun specially set up a Japanese restaurant on the third floor, and today he specially entertained guests with Japanese food. The two reporters were very disappointed. However, people in our country's press were very happy to taste foreign flavors.

The Establishment of Japanese Cuisine Japanese cuisine also has its own delicious flavors. Today, more and more people in our country are fond of Eastern flavors. However, they all have to go to Japanese restaurants in Hongkou, which are very expensive. People in our country suffer from this. Mr. Sun was aware of this, so he specially opened this department. This is the first time in Shanghai. The price is very low. So to recover the rights and interests, and to entertain Japanese news reporters, and to promote vigorously, so that even wooden clogs will gather here, then his intention is even deeper.

A Very Pitiful Reception There are female receptionists in the special elegant seats on the third floor. Among them, there are those who can speak Japanese. Mr. Sun asked me to test her level. After inquiring in detail, I learned that she was only twenty-eight years old. Her father used to do business in Yokohama, Japan, and was the chairman of the Chinese Zhicheng Association. He was quite famous for a time. Unfortunately, he died in the middle of the road. She drifted back to China and ended up as a female receptionist. When her father was alive, there were many guests and servants under his command. Therefore, her Japanese language is all used to address subordinates, not honorifics. However, in this career, it is necessary to use the most honorific language. Alas, the world is unreliable. Today's beggars may have been those whose carriages were filled with visitors in the past. I cannot help but speak out of emotion, so I also record it.

Trivial Talk on Silk Stockings

— Bing Lan

Clothing, food, and shelter are indispensable to life. Stockings, as daily necessities, also occupy an important position. In ancient times in our country, they were made of native cloth and called dubu stockings. Occasionally, they were made of Dutch standard cloth and called foreign cloth stockings. Later, Hong Kong thread stockings were imported and called foreign thread stockings. The size of these stockings was suitable for the feet, so everyone liked to use them. They were popular everywhere, and old-fashioned cloth stockings gradually became obsolete. In recent years, materials have evolved and science has flourished. As a result, there are silk stockings woven with electric machines. According to research, electric machines have been around in Europe and the West for more than ten years. In our country, it is still in its infancy. At that time, although there were more than ten families that purchased them, the new machinery was still a novelty, and it was inevitable that the technology was not refined and there was a lack of talent. As a result, it was a flash in the pan and gradually disappeared. Only a few companies, such as Nanyang Stocking Factory, remain. Nanyang was founded by Cantonese people. Cantonese people have always been known for their good management, so their performance is the best and their products are also refined. They are sold in various provinces and abroad, and their business is developing day by day. Moreover, Mr. Yu Chiring, the director of the factory, has rich knowledge of knitting. He studied in Germany. The recently invented small square heel, dance girl silk stockings, and 320-needle men's silk stockings are particularly distinctive. Mr. Yu said that this kind of small square heel silk stockings is already popular in Europe and the United States. In our country, it is still in its infancy. Now the results are quite good. He is very optimistic about the future of national goods.

Random Korean Musings (4)

— Jiping

Koreans are suffering from Japanese political and economic aggression. It is already extremely miserable. In addition, cultural aggression is a fatal wound to Koreans. Japan annexed Korea just over twenty years ago. Among Koreans under the age of thirty, whether male or female, those who are out of school are of course pitiful. But those who have the opportunity to study receive a slave education, which is even more pitiful. Most of those over thirty who have not received a slave education are still self-aware, believing that these young people are completely assimilated by Japan, which is indeed extremely dangerous. However, how many of these young people understand the advantages and disadvantages of this situation?

When I was in Seoul, I investigated the general situation of education in Korea. In Seoul, there is the Imperial University, as well as specialized schools for law, medicine, commerce, and industry, totaling four. There are fifteen secondary schools and over a hundred elementary schools. Most of them are run by the Japanese and, of course, implement their special educational policies. There are occasional schools established by Koreans themselves, but they must all follow the curriculum promulgated by the Governor-General's Bureau of Education. Courses mainly focus on Japanese, and the native Korean language, writing, and history are severely restricted. Therefore, most young students today speak fluent Japanese and write excellent Japanese. They even consider using Korean language to be backward and not as fashionable.

There are also special schools in Seoul and Pyongyang that are even more novel than American beggar schools, namely the so-called kisaeng schools. The purpose is to train outstanding female entertainers. The curriculum focuses on music, dance, social skills, and makeup. The course of study is stipulated to be four years. The students in these two schools are thriving, and their graduates occupy a significant position in the prostitution industry. The Japanese established such schools to cater to the psychology of social figures and as a policy to deal with Korea. They want to promote this kind of education, making the general public indulge in female allure, numbing the youth, and dividing the Korean spirit of striving for progress. The sharpness of their intentions is conceivable. A friend once told me, "Four or five years ago, Korea launched an independence movement. People everywhere showed fierce resistance. Students from the Pyongyang Kisaeng School also participated in the demonstrations." They also know that fighting for national freedom is much more glorious than the current majority of young people who are living a life of drunken stupor.

Saying Department Rotary Club

??? (21)

— Xu Zhuodai

How could Ziliang be willing to take it? If his own head doesn't hurt, why would he take headache medicine? There is no such reason. So he remained silent, not moving at all. His wife also felt that he couldn't take it and had to save him:

"If you don't take it now, you can take it in the evening!"

"This medicine is also very effective for menstrual pain!"

Ms. Ye said to his wife. The internal medicine was transferred to gynecology. Ziliang felt that categorizing his headache with menstruation was too impolite.

After a pause, Ms. Ye changed the subject:

"It's been less than a year since I came to Shanghai, and things are very different, Mr. Pan! Do you know mahjong? Can you take me somewhere to learn it? I feel like if I don't learn this thing, I'll definitely be left behind."

"To be honest, I don't know how to play."

Ziliang answered humbly, and his wife interjected:

"That foreign game is meaningless, just a temporary fad. I advocate promoting domestic products. Since you rarely come here today, let's play mahjong!"

Ziliang was extremely anxious. Playing mahjong would not only make it impossible to work today but might also drag others down, so he had to try his best to sabotage it:

"No, we don't have enough people!"

"We have three people here. We can invite Mrs. Jiang from next door, and that will make it four."

His wife suggested. Ziliang thought to himself, "I really can't escape, and they're going to invite Mrs. Jiang from next door." Mrs. Jiang is probably in her forties, and her voice is louder than a young Tatar. With these three ladies together, I won't be able to sleep tonight. Absolutely not! I'd better make up a lie:

"Mrs. Jiang went to Minhang this morning."

Gold Rush Rages Endlessly

18 taels and 9 qian higher than Saturday

Exceeding 50 Taels

Yesterday, the 13th, the gold standard suddenly soared. The market situation reached its peak, showing a momentum of advancing a thousand miles a day. The difference between the highest and lowest prices in the market was 15 to 16 taels. However, the fluctuations were not significant, with rapid advances and slow declines. As a result, the price surged by 19 taels. The industry's sentiment was high, but buying and selling were uneven. As for the silver market, it was reported to have fallen yesterday, probably because Germany's loan from England and France failed, and the gold price immediately soared. Subsequently, the foreign exchange rate still felt favorable, and the listed price also narrowed by one level. Therefore, it continued to rise upstream, with unparalleled sharpness. The buyers were agile, reaching 747-48 taels at one point. However, hedgers and others sold off, totaling about 34 taels. The market was stable and then declined again. Later, the exchange rate became even higher, and major players bravely competed to buy, causing the price to soar into the sky, actually approaching above 750 taels. The atmosphere in the market was very good. Today's forecast is that the main trend will continue to fall, with multiple parties working hard to raise the price, while the short sellers are under unexpected pressure.

Rumors of Unified Tax Treasury Bills to Be Auctioned

Issue Amount Estimated at 80 Million Yuan

The Twenty-Year Unified Tax Treasury Bills were issued on June 1st of this year, with an issue amount of 80 million yuan, for the purpose of supplementing the national treasury. The interest rate is 8%, with monthly repayment of principal and interest matters, to be cleared in 78 months, from June 20th to the end of November 26th, with interest decreasing along with the principal, and the amount of principal repayment gradually increasing each year. The fund is based on the surplus funds from the tobacco tax and cotton yarn wheat flour tax collected by the Ministry of Finance's Unified Tax Bureau, which are deposited daily in the Central Bank and managed by the Fund Management Committee. The face value is divided into four types: 5,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan. According to news from the Securities Market in this city, the Securities Exchange will soon open spot and futures trading for it, it is said.

Prices were one or two chi higher than in the previous market. Sales of mildewed glutinous rice were two less than arrivals, with no price changes.

South Market

Yesterday, arrivals were scarce, and transactions in urban and rural areas became more active. Su Tong's thick 粳 rice was bid up by one or two chi. Customers from Chongming and Hai'an inquired about Chang Xi's top-grade 粳 rice, but the quantities were small and sporadic, so the price only increased by one chi or so. Qingjiao, Si Song, Feng Lian, and other thin稻 rice continued to arrive, and sales were extremely good, with prices rising by two chi. Du Yang's rice market was tight, and after a long period of fatigue, sales were greatly boosted. Local retail sales were quite active, also up by one chi. Sales of the Tongbian mildewed rice were two less than arrivals, with a stable market. Although early rice was available on the market, the quantity was not large, and prices remained high. The amount of river clams opened was two or three thousand tan.

Mildew and Rain Drive Flour Prices Higher

Yesterday, the flour market generally trended towards firmness, due to continuous mildew and rain, causing various places to become swamplands, naturally affecting crops. As flour is also a staple food, outside investors were in a good mood, and buying interest was high. On the mill side, some mills had retracted recent positions, while others were selling distant positions. In Tianjin, only three yuan was sold for the soldiers' rations, with daily sales only reaching around 30,000. Sales of other brands were also flat, so this price increase had little to do with reality, but was only caused by the excessive flooding raising people's expectations. As a result, this month was 1.75% better than the previous week, August was 1.25% better, September was 1.5% better, October was 1.75% better, November was 1.25% better, and December was 1.5% better.

Sugar Market Trading Flat, Up One Mace and Strong

Yesterday, there were no telegrams from the sugar producing areas. The association's trading was flat, and due to the rising exchange rate, market sentiment was even better, and demand was strong. As the market rose, the transaction price for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was 10 taels, 0.085 to 0.09 yuan. High-quality, coarse-grained sugar was 11 taels and 0.05 yuan, and was scarce upon leaving the warehouse. The price was bid up to 11 taels and 0.01 yuan in the afternoon, and the trend was bullish. Japanese sugar prices also rose sharply, with N mark at 10 taels, 0.08 to 0.0875 yuan, and the highest price for new goods reaching 10 taels and 0.09 yuan. SH mark was 10 taels and 0.07 yuan, TM mark was 10 taels, 0.075 to 0.08 yuan, J mark was 11 taels and 0.02 yuan, TX mark was 10 taels, 0.0825 to 0.09 yuan, YT mark was 10 taels, 0.0775 to 0.085 yuan, and EZ mark was 10 taels and 0.055 yuan. Trading was very active, the market was firm, and there was a general trend towards a gradual rise.

North-South Goods, Xin Zhong Xing Vegetables Not Arrived Due to Rain

Xin Zhong Xing's daylily was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai today, but according to a telegram from Zhenjiang, due to continuous mildew and rain, it has not yet arrived in Zhenjiang. It is expected that it will not be available for three to five days. However, the harvest in the producing areas is abundant, and the market price in the future will definitely be flat. The Da Xing vegetables have not yet been weighed due to banditry in the producing areas and cautious observation by buyers, so the arrival will be further delayed.

Silk and Tea, Jiangsu Summer Cocoon Market Increasingly Sluggish

Jiangsu Production Almost Exhausted...Few Cocoon Shops Open

In the counties of Ningzhen, Changzhou, Wuxi, Chengxiang, and Suzhou in Jiangsu Province, the amount of summer silkworms raised this year was not weak. After the silkworm eggs hatched, the weather was sunny and warm, and the silkworms developed smoothly. However, during the major sleep stage, there was continuous mildew and rain, with sudden hot and cold spells, and silkworm diseases were rampant. Seven or eight out of ten silkworms suffered from black rot, yellow pus, and stiff paralysis. The cocoon production in various regions was almost exhausted, with statistics showing only one or two percent of a normal year's production. Moreover, due to excessive rainwater, the quality of the cocoons was generally poor. Cocoon shops in various regions have not officially opened, and Wuxi and other places are only receiving cocoons as they arrive. The highest price for cocoons is 50 yuan, with an average of about 40 yuan. This year's summer cocoons in Jiangsu Province are no longer marketable. The loss to farmers is even greater than that of spring silkworms, and everyone is complaining bitterly.

Overseas Silk Telegrams Not Transmitted

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign firm silk market was almost at a standstill. The European and American markets and Chinese silk mills were mostly inactive. Silk telegrams were not transmitted, and European firms suppressed prices and hoarded inventory. Chinese merchants were passive. Yesterday, only Kai Li imported five bales of Sichuan yellow factory silk and Samsung and others imported ten bales of yellow coarse silk, with prices remaining flat.

Needle Embroidery, Fine Eyebrow Tea Sales Active

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign firm tea market saw strong interest from French firms in needle embroidery, fine eyebrow tea, and other green teas arriving from various routes. There was also some activity in mid- to low-grade precious eyebrow and pearl tea. The overall market was quite active, but the selling price of Gongxi tea was consistently falling, becoming increasingly sluggish in recent days. The Russian firm's aid association is still indefinitely postponed, and the White Head firm has little appetite, with over 10,000 boxes already stockpiled in the market. There have also been no major transactions in black teas from Qining and other routes in recent days, and market prices are about 78 taels lower than before.

Metal Standards See a Resurgence of Price Increases

Although the metal market did not see any progress yesterday, prices rose again due to the tight exchange rate and high market sentiment. Eighteen-sheet black-headed skin was estimated at 11 taels and 5 mace per picul, and 70 to 80 piculs were opened yesterday, but there were more inquiries than before. Tinplate was also bid up by 0.025 yuan. British goods were 15 taels for 90 pounds, 15 taels and 0.075 yuan for 100 pounds, American goods were 16 taels and 0.075 yuan for 90 pounds, 17 taels and 0.035 yuan for 100 pounds, 200-pound company iron was 31 taels and 0.05 yuan, and 35-pound thin iron was 46 taels. Following the price increase, the market also offered Ma brand barrel heads at 4 taels and 0.045 yuan, bag heads at 4 taels and 0.005 yuan, and Elephant brand at 4 taels and 0.035 yuan (barrel heads), with bag goods estimated at 4 taels. White lead sheet, plain white iron, corrugated iron, and English steel plates all showed signs of prosperity. In short, recent changes in the metal market will depend on fluctuations in the exchange rate.

Book and Newspaper Introduction

Memoirs of Li Bu-lan

— Chun

Originally, literary figures often have love stories. Maeterlinck was no exception. When a woman he didn't know was infatuated with him after reading his work and expressed her love to him, and he happened to be in need of such things, he couldn't help but accept it. But who knew that after twenty years of marriage and cohabitation, they would divorce due to various misfortunes, each with a wounded heart, going their separate ways. For Maeterlinck, it may have been just a momentary impulse at the time, but for that woman, how could she have anticipated such a dramatic scene today? The protagonist is none other than Georgette Leblanc.

Li Bu-lan was deeply moved after reading Maeterlinck's famous works, *Princesse Maleine* and *Pelléas et Mélisande*, leaving a profound impression on her soul. She believed that the ideal character she had in mind was just like the characters described in those two books in terms of their personality and social status. As a result, she couldn't help but fantasize, and boldly expressed her love to Maeterlinck, eventually marrying him. This marriage, in anyone's eyes, would certainly be considered perfect. At the time, the literary and art circles widely spread the news, and countless people envied them. However, happiness ultimately turned to sorrow. The Maeterlinck in her ideal and the Maeterlinck after marriage were vastly different. In the end, she abandoned twenty years of cohabitation and agreed to a divorce.

Recently, Li Bu-lan, for some unknown reason, wrote a book, with a style similar to a memoir, openly describing the story of the combination of literary and marriage ties. However, the writing is quite calm and solemn, without revealing any frivolity, and even words of resentment are not lightly expressed. Although between the lines, she inevitably overflows with how different her impression of Maeterlinck after marriage is from her dreams before marriage. The description is very delicate, and the style is like her person. One wonders what Maeterlinck will think when he reads it. At the moment, this book has attracted the attention of the European and American literary circles.

Oriental Journal

— Chun

Tokyo, First Volume

Since the publication of the "Oriental Journal Kyoto First Volume" by the Kyoto Research Institute of Oriental Culture, it has attracted the attention of the general public. The Japanese are conducting such detailed research, ostensibly in the name of academic exploration, but there must be ulterior motives. However, their spirit is truly worthy of our admiration. They are not making efforts in superficial areas at all, and they are not afraid of difficulties in actually analyzing China's society, politics, economy, culture, geography, and history. They place even greater emphasis on tracing back Chinese history. Looking back at our own country, we are deficient, which is shameful. The organization of the Oriental Culture Institute is well-known because of its extensive activities in China.

The Tokyo Research Institute is one of its branches. The research is separate, but the affiliation is the same. The content of this Tokyo First Volume is roughly similar to that of the Kyoto First Volume. All the styles and titles are the same as the Kyoto volume. It is headed by Dr. Hattori Unokichi, Director of the Tokyo Research Institute. Now, the research topics of the seventeen researchers are listed below to show the general nature of their research projects:

Chinese Architectural Decoration – Ito Chuta

Historical and Chemical Research on Ancient Chinese Currency – Kato Shigeru, Domo Tsurumatsu

Research on Chu Ci Literature – Koki Sadakichi

Research on Successive Chinese Emperors – Go Ya Sadatakeshima Takuichi

Culture of the Khitans in Manchuria and Mongolia Before History and the Liao Dynasty – Torii Ryuzo

Correction of the Zheng Commentary on the Book of Etiquette – Hattori Unokichi

Restoration of the Tang Ordinances and Historical Research – Niida Noboru

Research on the System of Consciousness-Only Doctrine – Yuki Reimon

Ancient Central Asian Art (with special emphasis on painting) – Matsumoto Eiichi, Mitsugi Sasayoshi

Research on Chinese Family System (with special emphasis on the inheritance system) – Makino Tatsumi

Compilation of the Index to the Place Names in the Reading History to Survey the Territory – Aoyama Sadao

Compilation of the Illustrated Catalog of Ancient Chinese Artifacts – Harada Yoshito, Komai Kazuchika

The following articles are collected in this volume:

On the Various Alaya-Consciousness Theories in the Tang Dynasty Centered on the Treatise on the Establishment of Consciousness-Only – Yuki Reimon

A Study on the Year of Production of the Annotation to the Tang Law (Part 1) – Niida Noboru, Makino Tatsumi

Ancient Chinese Chemical Thought (Elemental Thought) – Domo Tsurusha

Shell Mounds Near Huanglong County, Shandong Province – Komai Kazuchika

Observing the Ancient State of Chu from the Perspective of Cultural History – Osa Kitasu

The report includes the establishment, current situation, and undertakings of the Research Institute, as well as Torii Ryuzo's lecture, "Travels in Manchuria and Mongolia." Each article has brilliant and unique insights. Such research is truly chilling to us.

Readers who want to know more about the content and observe its research achievements may wish to buy a copy. It is sold by Bunkyudo at 1-chome, Hongo, Tsujimoto-Hongo, Tokyo, Japan, and is priced at two Japanese yen. There is no Chinese translation available yet.

Finally, I would like to add one more sentence, that is, the reason why I want to provide this magazine is to hope that the Chinese academic community will not allow others to take the lead, and instead abandon our own things. How practical are their research topics!

Page 22

Art World

Recent World Art Scene

— Deming

Recent Trends in the French Art Scene

The French art scene has been in a relatively calm state recently. Even the Salon d'Automne, which has always been known for its revolutionary art, has shown signs of relaxation. Is this a good phenomenon or a bad one? We dare not make a hasty judgment. However, it is probably an inevitable trend to move from excessive excitement to fatigue.

Book Illustration

There is a bookstore owner in France named Ambroise Vollard. He has a great appreciation for art. He invites famous painters to create illustrations for famous literary works and publishes them. Thirty years ago, he printed two masterpieces by the great poet Verlaine. The illustrations were made by the great painter Bonnard. Now these two books have become rare editions. In addition, he has published several famous literary works illustrated by Rodin, Maurice Denis, and Bernard. Now he has invited several great painters such as Picasso, Rouault, Laprade, Dufy, and Chagall to collaborate on book illustrations. When these books are published in the future, they will surely become the most beautiful things in the publishing world.

"Three-Faced Views"

"Glaces à Trois Faces" is the name of a recent exhibition held in Paris. Why is it called "Three-Faced Views"? It turned out to be a collection of portraits of the same model by several painters, three by each person, and exhibited. The painters are the great Impressionists Renoir, Berthe Morisot, Mary Cassatt, Vuillard, and Despian. This exhibition is very interesting. From it, we see a very interesting point, that is, modern art pays attention to the subjective. Therefore, although the painters above painted portraits of the same model, the resulting portraits are not similar at all. If you ask several photographer-style painters to paint portraits of the same person, then the results they get will definitely be exactly the same.

New Buildings in the Berlin Museum

The Berlin Museum is the largest and most comprehensive museum in the world. Recently, many new buildings have been added there. This new construction began around 1901, designed and supervised by Alfred Messel, an architect at the time. Later, after Messel passed away, Ludwig Hoffman continued the construction. The project was suspended during the war. After the war, construction was resumed several years later. By the end of last year, all the buildings were completed. The most important of these new buildings are replicas of ancient Egyptian, Greek, and Roman buildings. The styles and sizes of these reproduced buildings are exactly the same as the originals. The purpose of this kind of construction is to allow people who do not have the opportunity to go to the locations of those ancient sites to appreciate their semblance. It is indeed needed by the public. However, this kind of construction is very expensive, and there are many difficulties in terms of engineering. Only the Germans have the courage to do it. People from other countries dare not try it easily.

New Art Institution in Poland

Recently, a new art institution has been established in Poland, called the "Society for the Promotion of Fine Arts." The purpose of that institution is to arouse public attention and understanding of various pure and applied arts. That institution started working in July last year. At that time, they held exhibitions in two lively summer resorts. However, their first important work was the recent exhibition of peasant art held in Warsaw. Peasant art is the art of the people, and it is of course the easiest to arouse public interest.

Finnish Architectural Art

The Finns pay extraordinary attention to architecture. There are several buildings there that can be said to be the most novel and outstanding in the modern architectural world. It turns out that that side is the embryonic land of futurist architectural art.

The most famous modern Finnish architect is Gottlieb Elieb Saarinen, who was born in Rantasalm in 1873. His masterpieces are the train stations in Hekingfors (Helsinki, the capital of Finland) and Wiborg. Lar Soncki is also an outstanding architect. The reason why the Finnish architectural school is famous all over the world and its influence extends to all countries is due to the work of those two great architects.

After Seeing the Works of the Students of the Shanghai Art College

— Chen Baoyi

This is the art exhibition of the graduating class of the Shanghai Art College in the twentieth year. It is a pity that the exhibition period is a bit late, but it is said that there are still quite a few enthusiastic people who brave the heat, sweat, and wander around the exhibition venue.

The exhibits are mainly the homework and graduation works of most of the students. Oil paintings account for the majority. In addition, for reference, there are some works by writers who have joined from outside, as well as several works by the professors.

The general situation of this art exhibition, I think, has been known to those who have visited, and it is natural that everyone has their own viewpoints… Now, I will just record a few words on my personal impressions of the works of the young people.

In Shanghai, it is a pity that there is no formal painting exhibition venue. Therefore, their works can only be displayed in the classrooms of the school. All the works are spread over six exhibition rooms of various sizes. Because there are so many points and the space is not enough, the distance between the paintings is inevitably too close. Visitors feel this shortcoming.

Most of the works give people a sense of brightness, which is slightly different from the gloomy works seen in the past. However, the so-called "tendency" is not like following military orders, doing the same work together in the same way, but seems to have the purpose of different paths leading to the same goal. Each person, according to their own qualities, is moving forward towards the vast "art journey." It also seems that when preparing for a difficult long journey, it is very important to pay attention to one's own health and physical strength. It seems that they are all aware of checking their "artistic health and physical strength."

Enough small talk, let's talk about their works.

Starting from the first room and looking at them in order... then Yang Taiyang's "Self-Portrait", Chen Zhuotang's "Still Life", Zeng Xiaolian's small "Nude" and "Landscape", Xie Chao's "Snow Scene", "North Station", Cui Zhenjie's pencil "Self-Portrait", HF Dai's "Dusk", Liao Feilai's "Bridge in Suzhou", "Suzhou Causeway", Li Zhongsheng's "Watercolor Still Life" (No. 3) "Oil Painting Still Life", Du Chaowen's "Landscape", Hu Changqi's "Lingyin Ancient Temple", Liang Xihong's "Landscape", "Dusk", "Flower Shop", Xia Yifang's "Landscape Next to the School", "In Front of the Courtyard"... Yong Tingguang's "Nude", "Spring in West Lake", Wang Shuren's "Nude", Du Shiqi's "After the Rain in West Lake", "Nude", etc., Zeng Zhiliang's "Nude with Socks", "ABC", "Little Rest", "Street", etc., Chen Zhuotang's "Flower", "Reclining Nude", etc., Yang Qiuren's "Self-Portrait", "Lake", "Maadolsne" and several other points, Yang Guangyang's "After the Rain", "Qixia Mountain Road", "Spring Painting" and several other points, and HF Dai's "Early Summer", "Corner of the Riverside", Liao Feilai's "Landscape of Hangzhou", etc. are all excellent works. There are several others, but it is too troublesome to describe them all, so I will omit them.

From the excellent works, you can also extract a few examples to briefly describe their characteristics...

Chen Zhuotang... likes to use dark and astringent colors. The so-called "dark and astringent color" here does not refer to a kind of gloomy and turbid color, but a kind of color that contains beautiful harmony in the dark and astringent. In terms of color tone, he seems to be groping for this kind of beauty. Works such as "Reclining Nude", "Flower", and "Still Life" all show this characteristic. In terms of expression, it is also straightforward and powerful.

In contrast to the above, there are the works of Yang Linren and Yang Taiyang. Although the styles of the two gentlemen are particularly different, they both use bright colors.

Yang Qiuren... the color tone is bright and beautiful without being mixed, showing a more delicate feeling. For example, the large "Lying Woman", "Self-Portrait", "Spring on Suzhou Causeway", River "Lake", etc. are examples for people to see.

Yang Taiyang... the color tone is bright and fresh, the brushwork is quite strong and has a Rhythmical momentum, and it has abundant power. For example, the nude depicted with Naples Yellow, full of Modele (flesh)... "After Drinking", and the use of large round brushstrokes to depict the moist green of trees and distant mountains, "Qixia Mountain Road", the picture is very thick and has a fresh feeling. In addition, such as "Male Image", "Little Rest", "Miss L", etc., all show their bright characteristics.

Du Shiqi... the brushwork is powerful and the colors have a beauty of calmness. Compared with the above examples, it has its own unique characteristics. Among his works, such as "After the Rain in West Lake", is painted with black and calm colors. The line drawing in the painting is quite beautiful and precise. The rest, such as "Landscape of West Lake", "Nude", etc., all show the writer's descriptive power.

Zeng Zhiliang's paintings also show bright and strong colors, and have a soft harmony. The brushwork is also careful. However, if he can pay attention to the "strengths and weaknesses" of expression, the effect will be better. Judging from his many works, it can be seen that he is also a diligent person who is rapidly improving. His works, such as "Street", "Little Rest", the large "Girl in Green Dress", "ABC", "Portrait of Sister" (1), etc. are all excellent works... In addition, there are several small works that seem to be futurist, but in terms of futurism, they are a bit weak.

My impressions of the works are as above. Regarding the other works, I will omit them.

…The study of art, of course, is to be tempered with "thought and technology." Because a painter is not just a painter who has only learned a little superficial skill... However, the field of painting is ultimately slightly different from the field of literature, that is, in terms of the "ideological and literary elements," in painting, I also feel that it is necessary to integrate or reflect those "elements" and "expression" into a painting's own "characteristics." It seems that simply focusing on the choice of "subject matter" is a different issue from "characteristics." Is this point to be considered?

The above is just a brief description of what I personally feel about the "works" from the "painting" point of view, so I have not specifically described the "subject matter" from a literary or ideological point of view, partly because my thoughts are very shallow.

Finally... from the works of the young writers seen this time, it is not difficult to predict the brilliance of their future. This is a gratifying thing. However, often due to self-satisfaction or other reasons, it is easy to give up halfway. This is something that we who study art have to pay attention to.
